{"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"type":"text","text":"Base directory for this skill: /config/.claude/skills/sc-task-unified-protocol\n\n> **NOTE**: Classification has already been performed by the `/sc:task` command before this skill was invoked. The classification header has already been emitted. Do NOT emit it again. This skill handles **execution only** for STANDARD and STRICT tier tasks.\n>\n> If for any reason no classification header was emitted before this skill was invoked, emit one now using ONLY the tier values STRICT, STANDARD, LIGHT, or EXEMPT (no other values are valid).\n\n# /sc:task-unified - Unified Task Execution with Compliance\n\n## Purpose\n\nUnified command that merges orchestration capabilities with MCP compliance enforcement. Automatically classifies tasks into compliance tiers and enforces appropriate verification.\n\n**Key Benefits**:\n- Single command replaces confusion between `sc:task` and `sc:task-mcp`\n- Automatic tier classification with confidence scoring\n- Appropriate verification for each task type\n- Prevents over-engineering for trivial changes\n- Ensures safety for critical changes\n\n## Triggers\n\nUse `/sc:task` when:\n- Task involves code modifications with downstream impacts\n- Complexity score >0.6 with code modifications\n- Multi-file scope (>2 estimated affected files)\n- Security domain paths detected (auth/, security/, crypto/)\n- Refactoring or system-wide changes requested\n\n**Auto-Suggest Keywords**:\n- High confidence: \"implement feature\", \"refactor system\", \"fix security\", \"add authentication\", \"update database schema\"\n- Moderate confidence: \"add new\", \"create component\", \"update service\", \"modify API\"\n\n## Usage\n\n```bash\n/sc:task [description]                           # Auto-detect all dimensions\n/sc:task [description] --compliance strict       # Force STRICT tier\n/sc:task [description] --compliance light        # Force LIGHT tier\n/sc:task [description] --skip-compliance         # Bypass compliance (escape hatch)\n/sc:task [description] --verify auto             # Auto-select verification\n```\n\n## Behavioral Flow\n\n### 0. Classification (Already Performed)\n\nClassification was handled by the `/sc:task` command before this skill was invoked. The tier has been determined and the classification header has been emitted. Proceed directly to execution based on the classified tier.\n\n**Reference** — the tier keyword tables (for context only, do not re-classify):\n- **STRICT**: security, authentication, database, migration, refactor, breaking change, encrypt, token, session, oauth\n- **EXEMPT**: explain, search, commit, push, plan, discuss, brainstorm\n- **LIGHT**: typo, comment, whitespace, lint, docstring, formatting, minor\n- **STANDARD**: implement, add, create, update, fix, build, modify, change (default)\n\n### 2. Confidence Display (Human-Readable)\n\nAfter the mandatory classification header, show a human-readable summary:\n\n```\n**Tier: STANDARD** [████████░░] 80%\n\nClassified as STANDARD:\n- Keywords matched: add, implement\n- Confidence score: 0.78\n- Considered alternatives: STRICT (0.35)\n```\n\nIf confidence <70%, add prompt: \"⚠️ Low confidence. Override with: `--compliance [strict|standard|light|exempt]`\"\n\n**Note**: The machine-readable header (Section 0) is for telemetry/A/B testing. This human-readable display is for user understanding.\n\n### 3. Execution Phase\n\nExecute task according to tier requirements:\n\n**STRICT Execution**:\n1. Activate project (mcp__serena__activate_project)\n2. Verify git working directory clean (git status)\n3. Load codebase context (codebase-retrieval)\n4. Check relevant memories (list_memories -> read_memory)\n5. Identify all affected files and test files\n6. Make changes with full checklist\n7. Identify all files that import changed code\n8. Update all affected files\n9. Spawn verification agent (quality-engineer)\n10. Run comprehensive tests: `pytest [path] -v`\n11. Answer adversarial questions\n\n**STANDARD Execution**:\n1. Load context via codebase-retrieval\n2. Search downstream impacts (find_referencing_symbols OR grep)\n3. Make changes\n4. Run affected tests OR document manual verification\n5. Verify basic functionality\n\n**LIGHT Execution**:\n1. Quick scope check (files/lines within bounds)\n2. Make changes\n3. Quick sanity check (syntax valid, no obvious errors)\n4. Proceed with judgment\n\n**EXEMPT Execution**:\n1. Execute immediately\n2. No verification overhead\n\n### 4. Verification Phase\n\nRoute to appropriate verification based on tier and paths:\n\n| Compliance Tier | Verification Method | Token Cost | Timeout |\n|-----------------|---------------------|------------|---------|\n| STRICT | Sub-agent (quality-engineer) | 3-5K | 60s |\n| STANDARD | Direct test execution | 300-500 | 30s |\n| LIGHT | Skip verification | 0 | 0s |\n| EXEMPT | Skip verification | 0 | 0s |\n\n**Critical Path Override**: Paths matching `auth/`, `security/`, `crypto/`, `models/`, `migrations/` always trigger CRITICAL verification regardless of compliance tier.\n\n**Trivial Path Override**: Paths matching `*.md`, `docs/`, `*test*.py` may skip verification.\n\n### 4.5 Test Failure Escalation Protocol (TFEP)\n\n**CRITICAL**: When tests fail during the Verification Phase (Section 4), agents MUST follow this protocol. Ad-hoc fixes are PROHIBITED.\n\n#### TFEP Prohibition Rules (VIOLATION-level)\n\nThese rules apply to ALL compliance tiers that run tests (STRICT, STANDARD):\n\n1. **VIOLATION**: Agents MUST NOT fix any code in response to test failures without completing the TFEP workflow.\n2. **VIOLATION**: Agents MUST NOT modify test expectations to make failing tests pass without adversarial validation.\n3. **VIOLATION**: Ad-hoc patches derived from test output are PROHIBITED. The agent must not read a traceback and immediately edit code to resolve it.\n\n**Permitted Exceptions** (MAY fix directly without TFEP):\n- Single `ImportError`/`NameError` in test scaffolding the agent just wrote, affecting <=2 tests, where the error is in the test file itself (not in implementation code).\n- Lint/formatting failures (trivially fixable, unambiguous root cause).\n- Deprecation warnings (not failures).\n\n**Valid Adversarial Outcome**: \"Test expectations are wrong\" is a legitimate conclusion from adversarial debate. When the debate concludes that test expectations are outdated rather than the code being wrong, this is NOT grounds for the agent to directly edit the tests — it must be presented to the user for review.\n\n#### Test Baseline Snapshot (Pre-Implementation)\n\nBefore implementation begins, the agent MUST record a test baseline:\n\n1. Capture the list of all existing test files and test function names at task start (e.g., via `uv run pytest --collect-only -q` or directory listing).\n2. Store this baseline in memory for the duration of the task.\n3. On any test failure, classify each failing test as:\n   - **Pre-existing**: Test name appears in the baseline (existed before this task).\n   - **New**: Test name does NOT appear in the baseline (written by the agent during this task).\n4. This classification drives the MUST-escalate vs MAY-fix-directly decision below.\n\n#### Escalation Trigger Detection\n\n**MUST escalate (trigger TFEP):**\n- Any **pre-existing test** fails (tests in the baseline that were not modified by the agent). This is the primary trigger — regressions in existing tests indicate the implementation broke something.\n- **3 or more new tests** fail simultaneously (indicates a systemic issue, not a simple typo).\n- **Runtime exceptions in implementation code** (TypeError, AttributeError, KeyError, etc. in the code being tested, not in the test scaffolding itself).\n\n**Escalation gradient (within-TFEP, for future forensic integration):**\n- Repeated failure (same test cluster fails after fix attempt) → escalate from light to standard\n- Multi-file blast radius from recent changes → escalate\n- Low-confidence root cause from adversarial debate → escalate\n- Unresolved adversarial outcome (no winner/tie) → escalate\n- Second failed retest → escalate\n- Cross-domain or non-obvious regression → escalate\n\n#### TFEP Execution Flow\n\nWhen TFEP triggers, execute the following steps:\n\n**Step 1: Halt and freeze**\n1. **STOP** testing immediately.\n2. **FREEZE** implementation — no further code changes permitted.\n\n**Step 2: Construct failure context**\n3. Build a `failure_context` YAML package containing:\n   - `test_names`: list of failing test function names\n   - `test_files`: list of test files containing failures\n   - `error_output`: full traceback/error output\n   - `expected_behavior`: what was expected\n   - `actual_behavior`: what actually happened\n   - `changes_made`: files changed during this task with descriptions\n   - `task_description`: current task description\n   - `test_baseline`: the pre-implementation test baseline\n   - `escalation_count`: which TFEP trigger this is (1, 2, or 3)\n4. Write context to `{output_dir}/context.yaml`.\n\n**Step 3: Invoke forensic**\n5. Determine the forensic tier based on escalation count:\n   - 1st trigger → `--tier light --intent triage`\n   - 2nd trigger → `--tier standard`\n   - 3rd trigger → **FULL STOP**. Report to user. Do not attempt further fixes.\n6. Invoke: `/sc:forensic --tier {tier} --intent triage --caller task-unified --context {context_path} --output {output_dir} --depth quick`\n7. The forensic pipeline runs autonomously through all its phases and returns a structured return contract.\n\n**Step 4: Consume forensic results**\n8. Read the forensic return contract from `{output_dir}/return-contract.yaml`.\n9. Handle based on status:\n   - If `test_is_wrong == true`: Present to user for review. Do NOT auto-fix tests.\n   - If `status == \"success\"`: Proceed to Step 5 (tasklist insertion).\n   - If `status == \"partial\"` or `recommended_escalation != \"none\"`: Increment `escalation_count` and return to Step 3.\n   - If `status == \"failed\"`: Report to user, halt execution.\n\n**Step 5: Tasklist insertion**\n10. Read `tasklist_insertion_path` from the return contract.\n11. Insert the remediation block into the current tasklist:\n    - Add `## Failure Remediation Plan (Adjudicated)` heading.\n    - Insert remediation tasks BEFORE existing test/verification tasks.\n    - Preserve original tasklist structure — append, don't replace.\n\n**Step 6: Resume**\n12. Resume execution with `--compliance strict` starting from the inserted remediation tasks.\n13. After remediation tasks complete, re-run the original test suite.\n14. If tests pass: TFEP resolved successfully. Produce incident report and continue.\n15. If tests fail again: Increment `escalation_count`, return to Step 2.\n\n#### TFEP Incident Reporting\n\nAfter each TFEP resolution (success or escalation), produce `tfep-incident-report.md`:\n\n```markdown\n# TFEP Incident Report\n\n- **Trigger**: {which threshold rule fired}\n- **Escalation count**: {1, 2, or 3}\n- **Failing tests**: {test names and classification}\n- **Root cause**: {summary from rca-verdict.md}\n- **Solution**: {summary from solution-verdict.md}\n- **Outcome**: {success / escalated / failed}\n- **Forensic artifacts**: {path to output_dir}\n```\n\nThis report is committed to git alongside other forensic artifacts.\n\n#### Escalation Budget\n\n```\n1st TFEP trigger  → /sc:forensic --tier light --intent triage    (~5-8K tokens)\n2nd TFEP trigger  → /sc:forensic --tier standard                 (~15-20K tokens)\n3rd TFEP trigger  → FULL STOP. Report to user. Do not attempt further fixes.\n```\n\n### 5. Feedback Collection\n\nAfter completion, collect implicit feedback:\n- Track if user overrode tier (implicit classification feedback)\n- Note smooth completion vs errors (quality signal)\n- Store for calibration learning\n\n## MCP Integration\n\n**Required Servers by Tier**:\n- STRICT: Sequential, Serena (fallback not allowed)\n- STANDARD: Sequential, Context7 (fallback allowed)\n- LIGHT: None required (fallback allowed)\n- EXEMPT: None required\n\n**Circuit Breaker Behavior**:\n- If required servers unavailable for STRICT tier, block task execution\n- For other tiers, use fallbacks with noted limitations\n\n## Tool Coordination\n\n**Planning Phase**:\n1. TodoWrite: Create task breakdown\n2. codebase-retrieval: Load context\n3. list_memories / read_memory: Check project state\n\n**Execution Phase**:\n1. Edit/MultiEdit/Write: Make changes\n2. Grep/Glob: Find references\n3. find_referencing_symbols: Trace dependencies\n\n**Verification Phase**:\n1. Task (quality-engineer): Spawn verification agent (STRICT only)\n2. Bash: Run tests directly (STANDARD)\n3. think_about_task_adherence: Reflect on completeness\n\n**Completion Phase**:\n1. write_memory: Save session state\n2. think_about_whether_you_are_done: Final check\n\n## Examples\n\n### STRICT Task\n```\n/sc:task \"implement user authentication with JWT\"\n\n-> Classified as STRICT (security domain, authentication keyword)\n-> Full 6-category checklist enforced\n-> Verification agent spawned\n-> Adversarial questions answered\n```\n\n### STANDARD Task\n```\n/sc:task \"add pagination to user list\"\n\n-> Classified as STANDARD (add keyword, typical feature)\n-> Context loaded before editing\n-> Downstream impacts checked\n-> Direct test execution\n```\n\n### LIGHT Task\n```\n/sc:task \"fix typo in README\"\n\n-> Classified as LIGHT (trivial keyword, documentation path)\n-> Quick sanity check only\n-> No verification delay\n```\n\n### EXEMPT Task\n```\n/sc:task \"explain how the auth flow works\"\n\n-> Classified as EXEMPT (explain pattern detected)\n-> Immediate execution\n-> No compliance overhead\n```\n\n### Override Example\n```\n/sc:task \"update config file\" --compliance strict\n\n-> User override to STRICT regardless of classification\n-> Full verification enforced\n```\n\n## Boundaries\n\n**Will:**\n- Classify tasks into appropriate compliance tiers\n- Enforce tier-appropriate verification requirements\n- Provide confidence scoring with rationale\n- Track feedback for continuous calibration\n- Support user overrides with justification\n\n**Will Not:**\n- Skip safety-critical verification for STRICT tasks\n- %s; creating fresh\", path)\n        return cls(path=path, release_id=release_id, spec_hash=spec_hash)\n\n    def begin_run(self, roadmap_hash: str) -> int:\n        \"\"\"Start a new run. Returns run_number.\"\"\"\n        from datetime import datetime, timezone\n        run_number = len(self.runs) + 1\n        self.runs.append({\n            \"run_number\": run_number,\n            \"timestamp\": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),\n            \"spec_hash\": self.spec_hash,\n            \"roadmap_hash\": roadmap_hash,\n        })\n        return run_number\n\n    def merge_findings(\n        self,\n        structural: list[Finding],\n        semantic: list[Finding],\n        run_number: int,\n    ) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Merge current scan findings into registry.\n\n        New findings: append with first_seen_run.\n        Known findings: update last_seen_run.\n        Missing findings: mark FIXED.\n        \"\"\"\n        current_ids: set[str] = set()\n\n        for source, findings_list in [(\"structural\", structural), (\"semantic\", semantic)]:\n            for f in findings_list:\n                stable_id = f.stable_id if hasattr(f, self.findings[stable_id][\"status\"] = \"ACTIVE\"\n                else:\n                    self.findings[stable_id] = {\n                        \"stable_id\": stable_id,\n                        \"dimension\": f.dimension,\n                        \"severity\": f.severity,\n                        \"description\": f.description,\n                        \"location\": f.location,\n                        \"debate_verdict\": None,\n                        \"debate_transcript\": None,\n                    }\n\n        # Mark missing findings as FIXED\n        for sid, finding in )\n        semantic_highs = sum(\n            1 for f in self.findings.values()\n            if f[\"status\"] == \"ACTIVE\" and f[\"severity\"] == \"HIGH\" and f[\"source_layer\"] == \"semantic\"\n        )\n        if self.runs:\n            self.runs[-1][\"structural_high_count\"] = structural_highs\n            self.runs[-1][\"semantic_high_count\"] = semantic_highs\n            self.runs[-1][\"total_high_count\"] = structural_highs + semantic_highs\n\n    def get_active_highs(self) -> list[dict]:\n        \"\"\"Return findings with status=ACTIVE and severity=HIGH.\"\"\"\n        return [\n            f for f in self.findings.values()\n            if f[\"status\"] == \"ACTIVE\" and f[\"severity\"] == \"HIGH\"\n        ]\n\n    def get_active_high_count(self) -> int:\n \"\"\"Read input files and return their contents as fenced code blocks.\n    71→\n    72→    Each file is wrapped in a fenced block with a ``# <path>`` header.\n    73→    Returns an empty string when _sanitize_output(output_file: Path) -> int:\n    86→    \"\"\"Strip conversational preamble and leading blank lines before YAML\n    87→    frontmatter in a step output file.\n    88→\n    89→    Reads the file, strips leading blank lines, finds the first ``^---``\n    90→    line, and removes everything before it.  Uses atomic write (write to\n    91→    ``.tmp`` then ``os.replace()``) to prevent partial file states.\n    92→\n    93→    Returns the byte count of the stripped content (0 when file already\n    94→    starts with ``---`` and has no preamble).\n    95→    \"\"\"\n    96→    import os\n    97→    import re\n    98→\n    99→    try:\n   100→        raw = output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   101→    except FileNotFoundError:\n   102→        return 0\n   103→\n   104→    # Strip leading blank lines (LLMs sometimes emit \\n\\n before ---)\n   105→    content = raw.lstrip(\"\\n\\r\\t \")\n   106→\n   107→    # Already starts with frontmatter delimiter -- no preamble to strip\n   108→    if content.startswith(\"---\"):\n   109→        if content == raw:\n   110→            return 0\n   111→        # Leading whitespace only -- write back the stripped version\n   112→        preamble_bytes = len(raw.encode(\"utf-8\")) - len(cleaned.encode(\"utf-8\"))\n   133→\n   134→    # Atomic write: tmp file + os.replace\n   135→    tmp_file = output_file.with_suffix(output_file.suffix + \".tmp\")\n   136→    tmp_file.write_text(cleaned, encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   137→    os.replace(tmp_file, output_file)\n   138→\n   139→    _log.info(\"Stripped %d-byte preamble from %s\", preamble_bytes, output_file)\n   140→    return preamble_bytes\n   141→\n   142→\n   143→def _inject_pipeline_diagnostics(\n   144→    output_file: Path,\n   145→    started_at: datetime,\n   146→    finished_at: datetime,\n   147→) -> None:\n   148→    \"\"\"Inject executor-populated pipeline_diagnostics into extraction frontmatter.\n   149→\n   150→    The LLM cannot reliably produce execution timing or environment metadata,\n   151→    so the executor injects these fields post-subprocess (FR-033).\n   152→    \"\"\"\n   153→    content = output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\").lstrip(\"\\n\\r\\t \")\n   154→    if not content.startswith(\"---\"):\n   155→        return\n   156→\n   157→    # Find end of frontmatter\n   158→    end_idx = content.find(\"\\n---\", 3)\n   159→    if end_idx == -1:\n   160→        return\n   161→\n   162→    # Idempotency: skip if already injected\n   163→    frontmatter = content[3:end_idx]\n   164→    if \"pipeline_diagnostics:\" in frontmatter:\n   165→        return\n   166→\n   167→    elapsed = (finished_at - started_at).total_seconds()\n   168→    diagnostics_line = (\n   169→        f\"pipeline_diagnostics: \"\n   170→        f\"{{elapsed_seconds: {elapsed:.1f}, \"\n   171→        f'started_at: \"{started_at.isoformat()}\", '\n   172→        f'finished_at: \"{finished_at.isoformat()}\"}}'\n   173→    )\n   174→\n   175→    # Insert before the closing ---\n   176→    new_content = content[:end_idx] + \"\\n\" + diagnostics_line + content[end_idx:]\n   177→    output_file.write_text(new_content, encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   178→\n   179→\n   180→def _inject_provenance_fields(\n   181→    output_file: Path,\n   182→    spec_source: str,\n   183→) -> None:\n   184→    \"\"\"Inject provenance fields into test-strategy frontmatter.\n   185→\n   186→    The test-strategy step's LLM output may omit provenance metadata\n   187→    (spec_source, generated, generator) since the prompt focuses on\n   188→    test strategy content. output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\").lstrip(\"\\n\\r\\t \")\n   192→    if not content.startswith(\"---\"):\n   193→        return\n   194→\n   195→    # Find end of frontmatter\n   196→    end_idx = content.find(\"\\n---\", 3)\n   197→    if end_idx == -1:\n   198→        return\n   199→\n   200→    # Idempotency: only inject fields that are missing\n   201→    frontmatter = content[3:end_idx]\n   202→\n   203→    fields_to_inject = []\n   204→    if \"spec_source:\" not in frontmatter:\n   205→        fields_to_inject.append(f\"spec_source: {spec_source}\")\n   206→    if \"generated:\" not in frontmatter:\n   207→        generated = datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()\n   208→        fields_to_inject.append(f'generated: \"{generated}\"')\n   209→    if \"generator:\" not in frontmatter:\n   210→        fields_to_inject.append(\"generator: superclaude-roadmap-executor\")\n   211→\n   212→    if not fields_to_inject:\n   213→        return  # All fields already present\n   214→\n   215→    provenance_block = \"\\n\".join(fields_to_inject)\n   216→    new_content = content[:end_idx] + \"\\n\" + provenance_block + content[end_idx:]\n   217→    output_file.write_text(new_content, encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   218→\n   219→\n   220→def _run_structural_audit(\n   221→    spec_file: Path,\n   222→    extraction_file: Path,\n   223→) -> None:\n   224→    \"\"\"Run structural audit as warning-only hook after EXTRACT_GATE pass (FR-EXEC.1).\n   225→\n   226→    Compares spec structural indicators against extraction requirement count.\n   227→    Logs a warning if extraction appears inadequate but never blocks the pipeline.\n   228→    \"\"\"\n   229→    from .spec_structural_audit import check_extraction_adequacy\n   230→    from .gates import _parse_frontmatter\n   231→\n   232→    try:\n   233→        spec_text = spec_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   234→        extraction_text = extraction_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   235→    except (FileNotFoundError, OSError) as e:\n   236→        _log.warning(\"Structural audit skipped: %s\", e)\n   237→        return\n   238→\n   239→    fm = _parse_frontmatter(extraction_text)\n   240→    if fm is None:\n   241→        _log.warning(\"Structural audit skipped: no frontmatter in extraction\")\n   242→        return\n   243→\n   244→    try:\n   245→        total_req = int(fm.get(\"total_requirements\", \"0\"))\n   246→    except (ValueError, TypeError):\n   247→        _log.warning(\"Structural audit skipped: unparseable total_requirements\")\n   248→        return\n   249→\n   250→    passed, audit = check_extraction_adequacy(spec_text, total_req)\n   251→    if not passed:\n   252→        _log.warning(\n   253→            \"Structural audit WARNING: extraction may be inadequate. \"\n   254→            \"Spec structural indicators=%d, extraction total_requirements=%d\",\n   255→            audit.total_structural_indicators,\n   256→            total_req,\n   257→        )\n   258→        print(\n   259→            f\"[roadmap] WARNING: Structural audit indicates possible extraction gap \"\n   260→            f\"(indicators={audit.total_structural_indicators}, requirements={total_req})\",\n   261→            flush=True,\n   262→        )\n   263→\n   264→\n   265→def _run_anti_instinct_audit(\n   266→    spec_file: Path,\n   267→    roadmap_file: Path,\n   268→    output_file: Path,\n   269→) -> None:\n   270→    \"\"\"Run the three anti-instinct detection modules and write audit report (FR-EXEC.3).\n   271→\n   272→    Invokes obligation scanner, integration contract checker, and fingerprint\n   273→    coverage checker deterministically (no LLM). Writes anti-instinct-audit.md\n   274→    with YAML frontmatter and markdown report body.\n   275→    \"\"\"\n   276→    from .obligation_scanner import scan_obligations\n   277→    from .integration_contracts import extract_integration_contracts, check_roadmap_coverage\n   278→    from .fingerprint import check_fingerprint_coverage\n   279→\n   280→    try:\n   281→        spec_text = spec_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   282→        roadmap_text = roadmap_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   283→    except (FileNotFoundError, OSError) as e:\n   284→        _log.error(\"Anti-instinct audit failed: %s\", e)\n   285→        raise\n   286→\n   287→    # Module 1: Obligation scanner\n   288→    obligation_report = scan_obligations(roadmap_text)\n   289→\n   290→    # Module 2: Integration contract checker\n   291→    contracts = extract_integration_contracts(spec_text)\n   292→    contract_result = check_roadmap_coverage(contracts, roadmap_text)\n   293→\n   294→    # Module 3: Fingerprint coverage\n   295→    fp_total, fp_found, fp_missing, fp_ratio = check_fingerprint_coverage(\n   296→        spec_text, roadmap_text\n   297→    )\n   298→\n   299→    # Build YAML frontmatter\n   300→    generated = datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()\n   301→    frontmatter = (\n   302→        \"---\\n\"\n   303→        f\"undischarged_obligations: {obligation_report.undischarged_count}\\n\"\n   304→        f\"uncovered_contracts: {contract_result.uncovered_count}\\n\"\n   305→        f\"fingerprint_coverage: {fp_ratio:.2f}\\n\"\n   306→        f\"total_obligations: {obligation_report.total_obligations}\\n\"\n   307→        f\"total_contracts: {contract_result.total_count}\\n\"\n   308→        f\"fingerprint_total: {fp_total}\\n\"\n   309→        f\"fingerprint_found: {fp_found}\\n\"\n   310→        f'generated: \"{generated}\"\\n'\n   311→        \"generator: superclaude-anti-instinct-audit\\n\"\n   312→        \"---\\n\"\n   313→    )\n   314→\n   315→    # Build markdown body\n   316→    body_parts = [\n   317→        \"\\n## Anti-Instinct Audit Report\\n\",\n   318→        f\"### Obligation Scanner\\n\\n\"\n   319→        f\"- Total obligations detected: {obligation_report.total_obligations}\\n\"\n   320→        f\"- Discharged: {obligation_report.discharged}\\n\"\n   321→        f\"- Undischarged (gate-relevant): {obligation_report.undischarged_count}\\n\",\n   322→    ]\n   323→\n   324→    if obligation_report.undischarged_count > 0:\n   325→        body_parts.append(\"\\n**Undischarged obligations:**\\n\")\n   326→        for o in obligation_report.obligations:\n   327→            if not o.discharged and not o.exempt and o.severity != \"MEDIUM\":\n   328→                body_parts.append(\n   329→                    f\"- Line {o.line_number}: `{o.term}` in {o.phase} \"\n   330→                    f\"({o.component})\\n\"\n   331→                )\n   332→\n   333→    body_parts.append(\n   334→        f\"\\n### Integration Contract Coverage\\n\\n\"\n   335→        f\"- Total contracts: {contract_result.total_count}\\n\"\n   336→        f\"- Covered: {contract_result.total_count - contract_result.uncovered_count}\\n\"\n   337→        f\"- Uncovered: {contract_result.uncovered_count}\\n\"\n   338→    )\n   339→\n   340→    if contract_result.uncovered_count > 0:\n   341→        body_parts.append(\"\\n**Uncovered contracts:**\\n\")\n   342→        for cov in contract_result.coverage:\n   343→            if not cov.covered:\n   344→                body_parts.append(\n   345→                    f\"- {cov.contract.id}: {cov.contract.description} \"\n   346→                    f\"({cov.contract.spec_location})\\n\"\n   347→                )\n   348→\n   349→    body_parts.append(\n   350→        f\"\\n### Fingerprint Coverage\\n\\n\"\n   351→        f\"- Total fingerprints: {fp_total}\\n\"\n   352→        f\"- Found in roadmap: {fp_found}\\n\"\n   353→        f\"- Coverage ratio: {fp_ratio:.2f}\\n\"\n   354→    )\n   355→\n   356→    if fp_missing:\n   357→        body_parts.append(\n   358→            f\"\\n**Missing fingerprints** ({len(fp_missing)}):\\n\"\n   359→        )\n   360→        for name in fp_missing[:20]:  # cap at 20 for readability\n   361→            body_parts.append(f\"- `{name}`\\n\")\n   362→        if len(fp_missing) > 20:\n   363→            body_parts.append(f\"- ... and {len(fp_missing) - 20} more\\n\")\n   364→\n   365→    content = frontmatter + \"\".join(body_parts)\n   366→    output_file.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n   367→    output_file.write_text(content, encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   368→\n   369→    _log.info(\n   370→        \"Anti-instinct audit complete: obligations=%d/%d uncovered_contracts=%d \"\n   371→        \"fingerprint_coverage=%.2f\",\n   372→        obligation_report.undischarged_count,\n   373→        obligation_report.total_obligations,\n   374→        contract_result.uncovered_count,\n   375→        fp_ratio,\n   376→    )\n   377→\n   378→\n   379→def roadmap_run_step(\n   380→    step: Step,\n   381→    config: PipelineConfig,\n   382→    cancel_check: Callable[[], bool],\n   383→) -> StepResult:\n   384→    \"\"\"Execute a single roadmap step as a Claude subprocess.\n   385→\n   386→    Builds argv with context isolation, launches process, waits with\n   387→    timeout, and returns StepResult.\n   388→    \"\"\"\n   389→    started_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   390→\n   391→    if config.dry_run:\n   392→        _log.info(\"[dry-run] Would execute step '%s'\", step.id)\n   393→        return StepResult(\n   394→            step=step,\n   395→            status=StepStatus.PASS,\n   396→            attempt=1,\n   397→            started_at=started_at,\n   398→            finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n   399→        )\n   400→\n   401→    # Anti-instinct: run deterministic audit directly, no Claude subprocess.\n   402→    # Gate evaluation happens via ANTI_INSTINCT_GATE in execute_pipeline.\n   403→    if step.id == \"anti-instinct\":\n   404→        spec_file = config.spec_file if hasattr(config, 'spec_file') else None\n   405→        merge_file = config.output_dir / \"roadmap.md\" if hasattr(config, 'output_dir') else None\n   406→        if spec_file and merge_file:\n   407→            _run_anti_instinct_audit(spec_file, merge_file, step.output_file)\n   408→        return StepResult(\n   409→            step=step,\n   410→            status=StepStatus.PASS,\n   411→            attempt=1,\n   412→            started_at=started_at,\n   413→            finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n   414→        )\n   415→\n   416→    # Wiring-verification: run static analysis directly, no Claude subprocess.\n   417→    # Returns PASS unconditionally; gate evaluation is handled separately by\n   418→    # the trailing gate runner (section 5.7.1).\n   419→    if step.id == \"wiring-verification\":\n   420→        from ..audit.wiring_gate import run_wiring_analysis, emit_report\n   421→        from ..audit.wiring_config import WiringConfig\n   422→\n   423→        wiring_config = WiringConfig(rollout_mode=\"soft\")\n   424→        source_dir = config.output_dir.parent if hasattr(config, 'output_dir') else Path(\".\")\n   425→        report = run_wiring_analysis(wiring_config, source_dir)\n   426→        step.output_file.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n   427→        emit_report(report, step.output_file)\n   428→        return StepResult(\n   429→            step=step,\n   430→            status=StepStatus.PASS,\n   431→            attempt=1,\n   432→            started_at=started_at,\n   433→            finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n   434→        )\n   435→\n   436→    # Inline embedding: read input files into the prompt instead of --file flags\n   437→    # --file is broken (cloud download mechanism, not local file injector) so\n   438→    # inline embedding is always used regardless of composed prompt size.\n   439→    embedded = _embed_inputs(step.inputs)\n   440→    if embedded:\n   441→        composed = step.prompt + \"\\n\\n\" + embedded\n   442→        if len(composed.encode(\"utf-8\")) > _EMBED_SIZE_LIMIT:\n   443→            # <= is intentional; _EMBED_SIZE_LIMIT = 120 KB is safely below MAX_ARG_STRLEN = 128 KB\n   444→            _log.warning(\n   445→                \"Step '%s': composed prompt exceeds %d bytes; embedding inline anyway\"\n   446→                \" (--file fallback is unavailable)\",\n   447→                step.id,\n   448→                _EMBED_SIZE_LIMIT,\n   449→            )\n   450→        effective_prompt = composed\n   451→        extra_args: list[str] = []\n   452→    else:\n   453→        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n   454→        extra_args = []\n   455→\n   456→    proc = ClaudeProcess(\n   457→        prompt=effective_prompt,\n   458→        output_file=step.output_file,\n   459→        error_file=step.output_file.with_suffix(\".err\"),\n   460→        max_turns=config.max_turns,\n   461→        model=step.model or config.model,\n   462→        permission_flag=config.permission_flag,\n   463→        timeout_seconds=step.timeout_seconds,\n   464→        output_format=\"text\",\n   465→        extra_args=extra_args,\n   466→    )\n   467→\n   468→    proc.start()\n   469→\n   470→    # Poll for cancellation while waiting\n   471→    while proc._process is not None and proc._process.poll() is None:\n   472→        if cancel_check():\n   473→            proc.terminate()\n   474→            return StepResult(\n   475→                step=step,\n   476→                status=StepStatus.CANCELLED,\n   477→                attempt=1,\n   478→                gate_failure_reason=\"Cancelled by external signal\",\n   479→                started_at=started_at,\n   480→                finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n   481→            )\n   482→        time.sleep(1)\n   483→\n   484→    exit_code = proc.wait()\n   485→    finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   486→\n   487→    if exit_code == 124:\n   488→        return StepResult(\n   489→            step=step,\n   490→            status=StepStatus.TIMEOUT,\n   491→            attempt=1,\n   492→            gate_failure_reason=f\"Step '{step.id}' timed out after {step.timeout_seconds}s\",\n   493→            started_at=started_at,\n   494→            finished_at=finished_at,\n   495→        )\n   496→\n   497→    if exit_code != 0:\n   498→        return StepResult(\n   499→            step=step,\n   500→            status=StepStatus.FAIL,\n   501→            attempt=1,\n   502→            gate_failure_reason=f\"Step '{step.id}' exited with code {exit_code}\",\n   503→            started_at=started_at,\n   504→            finished_at=finished_at,\n   505→        )\n   506→\n   507→    # Sanitize output: strip conversational preamble before gate validation\n   508→    _sanitize_output(step.output_file)\n   509→\n   510→    # Inject executor-populated fields into extract step frontmatter (FR-033)\n   511→    if step.id == \"extract\" and 514→        if hasattr(config, 'spec_file'):\n   515→            _run_structural_audit(config.spec_file, step.output_file)\n   516→\n   517→    # Inject provenance fields into test-strategy output\n   518→    if step.id == \"test-strategy\" and step.output_file.exists():\n   519→        spec_source = (\n   520→            config.spec_file.name if hasattr(config, \"spec_file\") else \"unknown\"\n   521→        )\n   522→        _inject_provenance_fields(step.output_file, spec_source)\n   523→\n   524→    # Process completed successfully; gate check happens in execute_pipeline\n   525→    return StepResult(\n   526→        step=step,\n   527→        status=StepStatus.PASS,\n   528→        attempt=1,\n   529→        started_at=started_at,\n   530→        finished_at=finished_at,\n   531→    )\n   532→\n   533→\n   534→def build_certify_step(\n   535→    config: RoadmapConfig,\n   536→    findings: list | None = None,\n   537→    context_sections: dict[str, str] | None = None,\n   538→) retry_limit=1,\n   571→    )\n   572→\n   573→\n   574→def _build_steps(config: RoadmapConfig) -> list[Step | list[Step]]:\n   575→    \"\"\"Build the 9-step pipeline with parallel generate group.\n 732→def _format_halt_output(results: list[StepResult], config: RoadmapConfig) -> str:\n   733→    \"\"\"Format HALT diagnostic output per spec section 6.2.\"\"\"\n   734→    failed = [r for r in attempt {r.attempt})' for r in passed) or 'none'}\",\n   764→        f\"Failed step:     {step.id} ({fail.status.value}, attempt {fail.attempt})\",\n   765→    ]\n   766→\n   767→    # Collect skipped )\n   787→\n   788→    return \"\\n\".join(lines)\n   789→\n   790→\n   791→def _get_all_step_ids(config: RoadmapConfig) -> list[str]:\n   792→    \"\"\"Get all step IDs in pipeline order.\"\"\"\n Returns:\n   897→        True if hash matches (fresh), False for any failure or mismatch.\n   898→    \"\"\"\n   899→    spec_deviations = output_dir / \"spec-deviations.md\"\n   900→\n   901→    # Case 1: spec-deviations.md not found\n   902→    if not spec_deviations.exists():\n   903→        _log.warning(\"Freshness check: spec-deviations.md not found\")\n   904→        return False\n   905→\n   906→    # Case 2: Read error\n   907→    try:\n   908→        content = spec_deviations.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   909→    except OSError as e:\n   910→        _log.warning(\"Freshness check: read error for spec-deviations.md: %s\", e)\n   911→        return False\n   912→\n   913→    # Case 3: Empty file\n   914→    if not content.strip():\n   915→        _log.warning(\"Freshness stripped.startswith(\"---\"):\n   921→        _log.warning(\"Freshness check: spec-deviations.md has no frontmatter\")\n   922→        return False\n   923→\n   924→    rest = stripped[3:].lstrip(\"\\n\")\n   925→    end_idx = rest.find(\"\\n---\")\n   926→    if end_idx == -1:\n   927→        _log.warning(\"Freshness check: spec-deviations.md has corrupt frontmatter\")\n   928→        return False\n   929→\n   930→    # Parse roadmap_hash from frontmatter\n   931→    saved_hash: str | None = None\n   932→    for line in rest[:end_idx].splitlines():\n   933→        line roadmap_hash field missing or empty\n   939→    if not saved_hash:\n   940→        _log.warning(\n   941→            \"Freshness check: roadmap_hash field missing or empty in spec-deviations.md\"\n   942→        )\n   943→        return False\n   944→\n   945→    # Case 6: roadmap.md not found\n   946→    if not roadmap_file.exists():\n   947→        _log.warning(\"Freshness check: roadmap.md not found at %s\", roadmap_file)\n   948→        return False\n   949→\n   950→    # Case 7: roadmap.md read error\n   951→    try:\n   952→        roadmap_content = roadmap_file.read_bytes()\n   953→ current_hash = hashlib.sha256(roadmap_content).hexdigest()\n   959→    if saved_hash != current_hash:\n   960→        _log.warning(\n   961→            \"Freshness check: hash mismatch -- saved=%s current=%s\",\n   962→            saved_hash[:12],\n   963→            current_hash[:12],\n   964→        )\n   965→        # FR-084: reset gate pass state for downstream steps\n   966→        if gate_pass_state is not None:\n   967→            for key in (\"spec-fidelity\", \"deviation-analysis\"):\n   968→                if key in gate_pass_state:\n   969→                    gate_pass_state[key] = False\n   970→        return False\n   971→\n   972→    return True\n   973→\n   974→\n   975→def _check_remediation_budget(\n   976→    output_dir: Path,\n   977→ 1255→\n  1256→\n  1257→def build_remediate_metadata(\n  1258→    status: str,\n  1259→    scope: str,\n  1260→    findings_total: int,\n  1261→    findings_actionable: int,\n  1262→    findings_fixed: derive_pipeline_status(state: dict) -> str:\n  1310→    \"\"\"Derive the overall pipeline status from state transitions.\n  1311→\n  1312→    State transitions at each boundary:\n  1313→    - post-validate: validated | validated-with-issues\n  1314→    - post-remediate: remediated\n  1315→    - post-certify: certified | certified-with-caveats\n  1316→\n  1317→    Returns one of: 'pending', 'validated', 'validated-with-issues',\n  1318→    'remediated', 'certified', 'certified-with-caveats'.\n  1319→    \"\"\"\n  1320→    certify = state.get(\"certify\")\n  1321→    if certify is not None:\n  1322→        if certify.get(\"certified\", False):\n  1323→            return \"certified\"\n  1324→        return \"certified-with-caveats\"\n  1325→\n  1326→    remediate = state.get(\"remediate\")\n  1327→    if remediate is not None:\n  1328→        return \"remediated\"\n  1329→\n  1330→    validation = state.get(\"validation\")\n  1331→    if validation is not None:\n  1332→        if validation.get(\"status\") == \"pass\":\n  1333→            return \"validated\"\n  1334→        if validation.get(\"status\") == \"fail\":\n  1335→            return \"validated-with-issues\"\n  1336→\n  1337→    return \"pending\"\n  1338→\n  1339→\n  1340→def write_state(state: dict, path: Path) -> None:\n  1341→    \"\"\"Write state dict to path atomically via tmp file + os.replace().\"\"\"\n  1342→    import os as _os\n  1343→\n  1344→    path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n  1345→    tmp = path.with_suffix(\".tmp\")\n  1346→ state from path with graceful recovery on missing/malformed files.\"\"\"\n  1352→    if not path.exists():\n  1353→        return None\n  1354→    try:\n  1355→        text = path.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n  1356→        if not text.strip():\n  1357→            return None\n  1358→        return json.loads(text)\n  1359→    except (json.JSONDecodeError, OSError):\n  1360→        return None\n  1361→\n  1362→\n  1363→def apply_decomposition_pass(deliverables: list[Deliverable]) -> list[Deliverable]:\n  1364→    \"\"\"Post-generation decomposition pass for the roadmap pipeline.\n  1365→\n  1366→    Runs after deliverable generation, before output formatting.\n  1367→    Splits behavioral deliverables into Implement/Verify pairs.\n  1368→\n  1369→    Idempotent: running twice produces identical results because\n  1370→    already-decomposed deliverables (IDs ending .a/.b) are skipped.\n  1371→\n  1372→    Preserves milestone-internal ordering: deliverables within each\n  1373→    milestone maintain their relative order after decomposition.\n  1374→    \"\"\"\n  1375→    return decompose_deliverables(deliverables)\n  1376→\n  1377→\n  1378→def _restore_from_state(\n  1379→    config: RoadmapConfig,\n  1380→    agents_explicit: bool,\n  1381→    depth_explicit: bool,\n  1382→) -> RoadmapConfig:\n  1383→    \"\"\"Restore agent/depth pipeline uses the same\n  1387→    configuration as the original run.\n  1388→    \"\"\"\n  1389→    state_file = config.output_dir / \".roadmap-state.json\"\n  1390→    state = read_state(state_file)\n  1391→    if state is None:\n  1392→        if not agents_explicit or not depth_explicit:\n  1393→            print(\n  1394→                \"WARNING: --resume with no state file found. \"\n  1395→                \"Using defaults for unspecified options.\",\n  1396→                file=sys.stderr,\n  1397→                flush=True,\n  1398→            )\n  1399→        _log.info(\"No state file found; using CLI agents for fresh run\")\n  1400→        return config\n  1401→\n  1402→    # Restore agents from state if user did not explicitly pass --agents\n  1403→    if not agents_explicit:\n  1404→        saved_agents = state.get(\"agents\")\n  1405→        if saved_agents and isinstance(saved_agents, list):\n  1406→            try:\n  1407→                restored = [\n  1408→                    AgentSpec(model=a[\"model\"], persona=a[\"persona\"])\n  1409→                    for a in saved_agents\n  1410→                ]\n  1411→            except (KeyError, TypeError) as exc:\n  1412→                _log.warning(\n  1413→                    \"Malformed agents in state file (%s); using CLI agents\", exc\n  1414→                )\n  1415→                return config\n  1416→\n  1417→            if restored != config.agents:\n  1418→                agent_str = \", \".join(f\"{a.model}:{a.persona}\" for a in restored)\n  1419→                print(\n  1420→                    f\"[roadmap] Restoring agents from state file: {agent_str}\",\n  1421→                    flush=True,\n  1422→                )\n  1423→            config.agents = restored\n  1424→        else:\n  1425→            _log.warning(\"State file has no agents key; using CLI agents\")\n  1426→\n  1427→    # Restore depth from state if user did not explicitly pass --depth\n  1428→    if not depth_explicit:\n  1429→        saved_depth = state.get(\"depth\")\n  1430→        if saved_depth:\n  1431→            if saved_depth != config.depth:\n  1432→      )\n  1440→            config.depth = saved_depth\n  1441→\n  1442→    return config\n  1443→\n  1444→\n  1445→def execute_roadmap(\n  1446→    config: RoadmapConfig,\n  1447→    resume: bool = False,\n  1448→    no_validate: bool = False,\n  1449→    auto_accept: bool = False,\n  1450→    agents_explicit: bool = True,\n  1451→    depth_explicit: bool = True,\n  1452→) -> None:\n  1453→    \"\"\"Execute the roadmap generation pipeline.\n  1454→\n  1455→    Builds the step list, handles --dry-run and --resume, then\n  1456→    delegates to execute_pipeline() with roadmap_run_step.\n  1457→\n  1458→    After all 9 steps pass, auto-invokes validation unless\n  1459→    --no-validate is set or --resume halted on a failed step.\n  1460→\n  1461→    Note: --no-validate does NOT skip the spec-fidelity step\n  1462→    (FR-010, AC-005). It only skips the post-pipeline validation\n  1463→    subsystem.\n  1464→\n  1465→    Args:\n  1466→        auto_accept: When True, the spec-patch resume cycle skips the\n  1467→            interactive prompt and proceeds automatically if evidence is\n  1468→            found. When False (default), the cycle prompts the user.\n  1469→            This is an internal parameter, not exposed on the CLI.\n  1470→        agents_explicit: Whether --agents was explicitly passed on the CLI.\n  1471→        depth_explicit: Whether --depth was explicitly passed on the CLI.\n  1472→    \"\"\"\n  1473→    config.output_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n  1474→\n  1475→    # On --resume with defaulted agents/depth, restore from state file\n  1476→    if resume:\n  1477→        config = _restore_from_state(\n  1478→            config,\n  1479→            agents_explicit=agents_explicit,\n  1480→            depth_explicit=depth_explicit,\n  1481→        )\n  1482→\n  1483→    # Apply hardcoded defaults for any still-None fields (non-resume or no state)\n  1484→    if not config.agents:\n  1485→        config.agents = [AgentSpec(\"opus\", \"architect\"), AgentSpec(\"haiku\", \"architect\")]\n  1486→    if not config.depth:\n  1487→        config.depth = \"standard\"\n  1488→\n  1489→    # FR-2.24.1.11: Recursion guard — local variable, per-invocation\n  1490→    _spec_patch_cycle_count = 0\n  1491→\n  1492→    # FR-2.24.1.9 Condition 3: Capture spec hash at function entry\n  1493→    initial_spec_hash = hashlib.sha256(config.spec_file.read_bytes()).hexdigest()\n  1494→\n  1495→    steps = _build_steps(config)\n  1496→\n  1497→    # --dry-run: print plan and exit\n  1498→    if config.dry_run:\n  1499→        _dry_run_output(steps)\n  1500→        return\n  1501→\n  1502→    # --resume: check which steps already pass their gates\n  1503→    if resume:\n  1504→        from ..pipeline.gates import gate_passed\n  1505→\n  1506→        steps = _apply_resume(steps, config, gate_passed)\n  1507→\n  1508→    # Execute pipeline\n  1509→    results = execute_pipeline(\n  1510→        steps=steps,\n  1511→        config=config,\n  1512→        run_step=roadmap_run_step,\n  1513→        on_step_start=_print_step_start,\n  1514→        on_step_complete=_print_step_complete,\n  1515→    )\n  1516→\n  1517→    # Save state\n  1518→    _save_state(config, results)\n  1519→\n  1520→    # Check for failures\n  1521→    failures = [r for r in results if r.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT)]\n  1522→    if failures:\n  1523→        # FR-2.24.1.9: Check if spec-fidelity failed and auto-resume is possible\n  1524→        spec_fidelity_failed = any(\n  1525→            r.step\n  1526→            and r.step.id == \"spec-fidelity\"\n  1527→            and r.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT)\n  1528→            for r in results\n  1529→        )\n  1530→\n  1531→        if spec_fidelity_failed:\n  1532→            resumed = _apply_resume_after_spec_patch(\n  1533→                config=config,\n  1534→                results=results,\n  1535→                auto_accept=auto_accept,\n  1536→                initial_spec_hash=initial_spec_hash,\n  1537→                cycle_count=_spec_patch_cycle_count,\n  1538→            )\n  1539→            if resumed:\n  1540→                _spec_patch_cycle_count += 1\n  1541→                # Cycle complete — resumed pipeline ran to completion or failure\n  1542→                # inside _apply_resume_after_spec_patch. If it returned True,\n  1543→                # we're done (either success or failure was handled internally).\n  1544→                return\n  1545→\n  1546→        halt_msg = _format_halt_output(results, config)\n  1547→        print(halt_msg, file=sys.stderr)\n  1548→        sys.exit(1)\n  1549→\n  1550→    print(f\"\\n[roadmap] Pipeline complete: {len(results)} steps passed\", flush=True)\n  1551→\n  1552→    # Auto-invoke validation after successful pipeline completion\n  1553→    if no_validate:\n  1554→        print(\"[roadmap] Validation skipped (--no-validate)\", flush=True)\n  1555→        _save_validation_status(config, \"skipped\")\n  1556→        return\n  1557→\n  1558→    # Check if validation already completed (--resume path)\n  1559→    if resume:\n  1560→        state_file = config.output_dir / \".roadmap-state.json\"\n  1561→        state = read_state(state_file)\n  1562→        if state and \"validation\" in state:\n  1563→            saved = state[\"validation\"]\n  1564→            if saved.get(\"status\") in (\"pass\", \"fail\"):\n  1565→                print(\n  1566→                    f\"[roadmap] Validation already completed ({saved['status']}), skipping\",\n  1567→                    flush=True,\n  1568→                )\n  1569→                return\n  1570→\n  1571→    _auto_invoke_validate(config)\n  1572→\n  1573→\n  1574→def _find_qualifying_deviation_files(\n  1575→    config: RoadmapConfig,\n  1576→    results: list[StepResult],\n  1577→) -> list:\n  1578→    \"\"\"Find deviation files written after spec-fidelity started.\n  1579→\n  1580→    Returns qualifying DeviationRecord objects, or empty list if\n  1581→    conditions are not met.\n  1582→\n  1583→    Implementation detail — not specified in the spec. Extracted for\n  1584→    testability of the three-condition detection gate.\n  1585→    \"\"\"\n  1586→    from .spec_patch import scan_accepted_deviation_records\n  1587→\n  1588→    state_file = config.output_dir / \".roadmap-state.json\"\n  1589→    state = read_state(state_file)\n  1590→    if state is None:\n  1591→        return []\n  1592→\n  1593→    # Get spec-fidelity started_at timestamp\n  1594→    steps_state = state.get(\"steps\", {})\n  1595→    fidelity_state = steps_state.get(\"spec-fidelity\", {})\n  1596→    started_at_str = fidelity_state.get(\"started_at\")\n  1597→\n  1598→    # Fail-closed: if started_at is absent, condition not met\n  1599→    if not started_at_str:\n  1600→        return []\n  1601→\n  1602→    try:\n  1603→        started_at_ts = datetime.fromisoformat(started_at_str).timestamp()\n  1604→    except (ValueError, TypeError):\n  1605→        return []\n  1606→\n  1607→    # Scan all deviation records\n  1608→    all_records = scan_accepted_deviation_records(config.output_dir)\n  1609→    if not all_records:\n  1610→        return []\n  1611→\n  1612→    # Filter to records written AFTER spec-fidelity started.\n  1613→    # Strict > (not >=): a record with mtime == started_at was written before\n  1614→    # or exactly at step start, so it cannot be evidence of a subprocess fix.\n  1615→    # Caveat: HFS+ and some NFS mounts have 1-second mtime resolution, so\n  1616→    # records created within the same second as started_at may be missed.\n  1617→    qualifying = [r for r in all_records if r.mtime > started_at_ts]\n  1618→    return qualifying\n  1619→\n  1620→\n  1621→def _apply_resume_after_spec_patch(\n  1622→    config: RoadmapConfig,\n  1623→    results: list[StepResult],\n  1624→    auto_accept: bool,\n  1625→    initial_spec_hash: str,\n  1626→    cycle_count: int,\n  1627→) -> bool:\n  1628→    \"\"\"Attempt a single spec-patch auto-resume cycle after spec-fidelity FAIL.\n  1629→\n  1630→    Evaluates the three-condition detection gate (FR-2.24.1.9):\n  1631→      1. Recursion guard: cycle_count == 0\n  1632→      2. Qualifying deviation files exist with mtime > started_at\n  1633→      3. Spec file hash changed since run started (initial_spec_hash)\n  1634→\n  1635→    If all conditions pass, executes the six-step disk-reread sequence\n  1636→    (FR-2.24.1.10) and re-runs the pipeline via _apply_resume.\n  1637→\n  1638→    Single-writer assumption: no concurrent writer modifies\n  1639→    .roadmap-state.json between the reread and write steps.\n  1640→\n  1641→    Returns True if the cycle was attempted (regardless of outcome),\n  1642→    False if conditions were not met.\n  1643→    \"\"\"\n  1644→    # FR-2.24.1.11: Recursion guard\n  1645→    if cycle_count >= 1:\n  1646→        print(\n  1647→            \"[roadmap] Spec-patch cycle already exhausted \"\n  1648→            f\"(cycle_count={cycle_count}). Proceeding to normal failure.\",\n  1649→            flush=True,\n  1650→        )\n  1651→        return False\n  1652→\n  1653→    # FR-2.24.1.9 Condition 2: Qualifying deviation files\n  1654→    qualifying = _find_qualifying_deviation_files(config, results)\n  1655→    if not qualifying:\n  1656→        return False\n  1657→\n  1658→    # FR-2.24.1.9 Condition 3: Spec hash changed since run started\n  1659→    current_hash = hashlib.sha256(config.spec_file.read_bytes()).hexdigest()\n  1660→    if current_hash == initial_spec_hash:\n  1661→        return False\n  1662→\n  1663→    # All three conditions met — enter the cycle\n  1664→    # FR-2.24.1.12: Cycle entry logging\n  1665→    print(\n  1666→        f\"[roadmap] Spec patched by subprocess. \"\n  1667→        f\"Found {len(qualifying)} accepted deviation record(s).\",\n  1668→        flush=True,\n  1669→    )\n  1670→    print(\n  1671→        \"[roadmap] Triggering spec-hash sync and resume (cycle 1/1).\",\n  1672→        flush=True,\n  1673→    )\n  1674→\n  1675→    # FR-2.24.1.10: Six-step disk-reread sequence\n  1676→    state_file = config.output_dir / \".roadmap-state.json\"\n  1677→\n  1678→    # Step 1: Re-read state from disk\n  1679→    _fresh_state = read_state(state_file)  # noqa: F841\n  1680→\n  1681→    # Step 2: Recompute spec hash\n  1682→    new_hash = hashlib.sha256(config.spec_file.read_bytes()).hexdigest()\n  1683→\n  1684→    # Step 3: Atomic write of new hash\n  1685→    try:\n  1686→        # Read again for fresh copy, update only spec_hash, write atomically\n  1687→        fresh_for_write = read_state(state_file) or {}\n  1688→        fresh_for_write[\"spec_hash\"] = new_hash\n  1689→        write_state(fresh_for_write, state_file)\n  1690→    except OSError as exc:\n  1691→        print(\n  1692→            f\"[roadmap] ERROR: Failed to update spec_hash during \"\n  1693→            f\"auto-resume cycle: {exc}. Falling through to normal failure.\",\n  1694→            file=sys.stderr,\n  1695→            flush=True,\n  1696→        )\n  1697→        return True  # Cycle was attempted but failed — don't retry\n  1698→\n  1699→    # Step 4: Re-read state from disk AGAIN (this is what _apply_resume gets)\n  1700→    post_write_state = read_state(state_file)\n  1701→    if post_write_state is None:\n  1702→        print(\n  1703→            \"[roadmap] ERROR: Could not re-read state after write. \"\n  1704→            \"Falling through to normal failure.\",\n  1705→            file=sys.stderr,\n  1706→            flush=True,\n  1707→        )\n  1708→        return True\n  1709→\n  1710→    # Step 5: Rebuild steps\n  1711→    steps = _build_steps(config)\n  1712→\n  1713→    # Step 6: Apply resume with post-write state\n  1714→    from ..pipeline.gates import gate_passed\n  1715→\n  1716→    steps = _apply_resume(steps, config, gate_passed)\n  1717→\n  1718→    # Re-execute pipeline from the resumed point\n  1719→    resumed_results = execute_pipeline(\n  1720→        steps=steps,\n  1721→        config=config,\n  1722→        run_step=roadmap_run_step,\n  1723→        on_step_start=_print_step_start,\n  1724→        on_step_complete=_print_step_complete,\n  1725→    )\n  1726→\n  1727→    # Save state from resumed run\n  1728→    _save_state(config, resumed_results)\n  1729→\n  1730→    # FR-2.24.1.12: Cycle completion logging\n  1731→    print(\"[roadmap] Spec-patch resume cycle complete.\", flush=True)\n  1732→\n  1733→    # Check if resumed pipeline also failed\n  1734→    resumed_failures = [\n  1735→        r for r in resumed_results if r.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT)\n  1736→    ]\n  1737→    if resumed_failures:\n  1738→        # Module 1: Obligation scanner\n    obligation_report = scan_obligations(roadmap_text)\n\n    # Module 2: Integration contract checker\n    contracts = extract_integration_contracts(spec_text)\n    contract_result = check_roadmap_coverage(contracts, roadmap_text)\n\n    # Module 3: Fingerprint coverage\n    fp_total, fp_found, fp_missing, fp_ratio = check_fingerprint_coverage(\n        spec_text, roadmap_text\n    )\n\n    # Build YAML frontmatter\n    generated = datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()\n    frontmatter = (\n        \"---\\n\"\n        f\"undischarged_obligations: {obligation_report.undischarged_count}\\n\"\n        f\"uncovered_contracts: {contract_result.uncovered_count}\\n\"\n        f\"fingerprint_coverage: {fp_ratio:.2f}\\n\"\n        f\"total_obligations: {obligation_report.total_obligations}\\n\"\n        f\"total_contracts: {contract_result.total_count}\\n\"\n        f\"fingerprint_total: {fp_total}\\n\"\n        f\"fingerprint_found: {fp_found}\\n\"\n        f'generated: \"{generated}\"\\n'\n        \"generator: superclaude-anti-instinct-audit\\n\"\n        \"---\\n\"\n    )\n\n    # Build markdown body\n    body_parts = [\n        \"\\n## Anti-Instinct Audit Report\\n\",\n        f\"### Obligation Scanner\\n\\n\"\n        f\"- Total obligations detected: {obligation_report.total_obligations}\\n\"\n        f\"- Discharged: {obligation_report.discharged}\\n\"\n        f\"- Undischarged (gate-relevant): {obligation_report.undischarged_count}\\n\",\n    ]\n\n    if obligation_report.undischarged_count > 0:\n        body_parts.append(\"\\n**Undischarged obligations:**\\n\")\n        for o in obligation_report.obligations:\n            if not o.discharged and not o.exempt and o.severity != \"MEDIUM\":\n                body_parts.append(\n                    f\"- Line {o.line_number}: `{o.term}` in {o.phase} \"\n                    f\"({o.component})\\n\"\n                )\n\n    body_parts.append(\n        f\"\\n### Integration Contract Coverage\\n\\n\"\n        f\"- Total contracts: {contract_result.total_count}\\n\"\n        f\"- Covered: {contract_result.total_count - contract_result.uncovered_count}\\n\"\n        f\"- Uncovered: {contract_result.uncovered_count}\\n\"\n    )\n\n    if contract_result.uncovered_count > 0:\n        body_parts.append(\"\\n**Uncovered contracts:**\\n\")\n        for cov in contract_result.coverage:\n            if not cov.covered:\n                body_parts.append(\n                    f\"- {cov.contract.id}: {cov.contract.description} \"\n                    f\"({cov.contract.spec_location})\\n\"\n                )\n\n    body_parts.append(\n        f\"\\n### Fingerprint Coverage\\n\\n\"\n        f\"- Total fingerprints: {fp_total}\\n\"\n        f\"- Found in roadmap: {fp_found}\\n\"\n        f\"- Coverage ratio: {fp_ratio:.2f}\\n\"\n    )\n\n    if fp_missing:\n        body_parts.append(\n            f\"\\n**Missing fingerprints** ({len(fp_missing)}):\\n\"\n        )\n        for name in fp_missing[:20]:  # cap at 20 for readability\n            body_parts.append(f\"- `{name}`\\n\")\n        if len(fp_missing) > 20:\n            body_parts.append(f\"- ... and {len(fp_missing) - 20} more\\n\")\n\n    content = frontmatter + \"\".join(body_parts)\n    output_file.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n    output_file.write_text(content, encoding=\"utf-8\")\n\n    _log.info(\n        \"Anti-instinct audit complete: obligations=%d/%d uncovered_contracts=%d \"\n        \"fingerprint_coverage=%.2f\",\n        obligation_report.undischarged_count,\n        obligation_report.total_obligations,\n        contract_result.uncovered_count,\n        fp_ratio,\n    )\n\n\ndef roadmap_run_step(\n    step: Step,\n    config: PipelineConfig,\n    cancel_check: Callable[[], bool],\n) -> StepResult:\n    \"\"\"Execute a single roadmap step as a Claude subprocess.\n\n    Builds argv with context isolation, launches process, waits with\n    timeout, and returns StepResult.\n    \"\"\"\n    started_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n\n    if config.dry_run:\n        _log.info(\"[dry-run] Would execute step '%s'\", step.id)\n        return StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.PASS,\n            attempt=1,\n            started_at=started_at,\n            finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n        )\n\n    # Anti-instinct: run deterministic audit directly, no Claude subprocess.\n    # Gate evaluation happens via ANTI_INSTINCT_GATE in execute_pipeline.\n    if step.id == \"anti-instinct\":\n        spec_file = config.spec_file if hasattr(config, 'spec_file') else None\n        merge_file = config.output_dir / \"roadmap.md\" if hasattr(config, 'output_dir') else None\n        if spec_file and merge_file:\n            _run_anti_instinct_audit(spec_file, merge_file, step.output_file)\n        return StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.PASS,\n            attempt=1,\n            started_at=started_at,\n            finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n        )\n\n    # Wiring-verification: run static analysis directly, no Claude subprocess.\n    # Returns PASS unconditionally; gate evaluation is handled separately by\n    # the trailing gate runner (section 5.7.1).\n    if step.id == \"wiring-verification\":\n        from ..audit.wiring_gate import run_wiring_analysis, emit_report\n        from ..audit.wiring_config import WiringConfig\n\n        wiring_config = WiringConfig(rollout_mode=\"soft\")\n        source_dir = config.output_dir.parent if hasattr(config, 'output_dir') else Path(\".\")\n        report = run_wiring_analysis(wiring_config, source_dir)\n        step.output_file.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n        emit_report(report, step.output_file)\n        return StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.PASS,\n            attempt=1,\n            started_at=started_at,\n            finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n        )\n\n    # Inline embedding: read input files into the prompt instead of --file flags\n    # --file is broken (cloud download mechanism, not local file injector) so\n    # inline embedding is always used regardless of composed prompt size.\n    embedded = _embed_inputs(step.inputs)\n    if embedded:\n        composed = step.prompt + \"\\n\\n\" + embedded\n        if len(composed.encode(\"utf-8\")) > _EMBED_SIZE_LIMIT:\n            # <= is intentional; _EMBED_SIZE_LIMIT = 120 KB is safely below MAX_ARG_STRLEN = 128 KB\n            _log.warning(\n                \"Step '%s': composed prompt exceeds %d bytes; embedding inline anyway\"\n                \" (--file fallback is unavailable)\",\n                step.id,\n                _EMBED_SIZE_LIMIT,\n            )\n        effective_prompt = composed\n        extra_args: list[str] = []\n    else:\n        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n        extra_args = []\n\n    proc = ClaudeProcess(\n        prompt=effective_prompt,\n        output_file=step.output_file,\n        error_file=step.output_file.with_suffix(\".err\"),\n        max_turns=config.max_turns,\n        model=step.model or config.model,\n        permission_flag=config.permission_flag,\n        timeout_seconds=step.timeout_seconds,\n        output_format=\"text\",\n        extra_args=extra_args,\n    )\n\n    proc.start()\n\n    # Poll for cancellation while waiting\n    while proc._process is not None and proc._process.poll() is None:\n        if cancel_check():\n            proc.terminate()\n            return StepResult(\n                step=step,\n                status=StepStatus.CANCELLED,\n                attempt=1,\n                gate_failure_reason=\"Cancelled by external signal\",\n                started_at=started_at,\n                finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n            )\n        time.sleep(1)\n\n    exit_code = proc.wait()\n    finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n\n    if exit_code == 124:\n        return StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.TIMEOUT,\n            attempt=1,\n            gate_failure_reason=f\"Step '{step.id}' timed out after {step.timeout_seconds}s\",\n            started_at=started_at,\n            finished_at=finished_at,\n        )\n\n    if exit_code != 0:\n        return StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.FAIL,\n            attempt=1,\n            gate_failure_reason=f\"Step '{step.id}' exited with code {exit_code}\",\n            started_at=started_at,\n            finished_at=finished_at,\n        )\n\n    # Sanitize output: strip conversational preamble before gate validation\n    _sanitize_output(step.output_file)\n\n    # Inject executor-populated fields into extract step frontmatter (FR-033)\n    if step.id == \"extract\" and step.output_file.exists():\n        _inject_pipeline_diagnostics(step.output_file, started_at, finished_at)\n        # FR-EXEC.1: Structural audit hook (warning-only, never blocks)\n        if hasattr(config, 'spec_file'):\n            _run_structural_audit(config.spec_file, step.output_file)\n\n    # Inject provenance fields into test-strategy output\n    if step.id == \"test-strategy\" and step.output_file.exists():\n        spec_source = (\n            config.spec_file.name if hasattr(config, \"spec_file\") else \"unknown\"\n        )\n        _inject_provenance_fields(step.output_file, spec_source)\n\n    # Process completed successfully; gate check happens in execute_pipeline\n    return StepResult(\n        step=step,\n        status=StepStatus.PASS,\n        attempt=1,\n        started_at=started_at,\n        finished_at=finished_at,\n    )\n\n\ndef build_certify_step(\n    config: RoadmapConfig,\n    findings: list | None = None,\n    context_sections: dict[str, str] | None = None,\n) -> Step:\n    \"\"\"Build a certify Step for execution via execute_pipeline().\n\n    The certify step runs as a standard Step (not ClaudeProcess directly)\n    per spec section 2.5. HALT diagnostic output per spec section 6.2.\"\"\"\n    failed = [r for r in results if r.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT)]\n    passed = [r for r in results if r.status == StepStatus.PASS]\n    cancelled = [r for r in results if r.status == StepStatus.CANCELLED]\n\n    if not failed:\n        return \"\"\n\n    fail = failed[-1]\n    step = fail.step\n\n    # Calculate file details if output exists\n    file_info = \"\"\n    if step and step.output_file.exists():\n        content = step.output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n        byte_count = len(content.encode(\"utf-8\"))\n        line_count = len(content.splitlines())\n        file_info = f\"  Output size: {byte_count} bytes ({line_count} lines)\\n\"\n    elif step:\n        file_info = \"  Output file: not created\\n\"\n\n    elapsed = f\"{fail.duration_seconds:.0f}s\"\n\n    lines = [\n        f\"ERROR: Roadmap pipeline halted at step '{step.id}' (attempt {fail.attempt}/2)\",\n        f\"  Gate failure: {fail.gate_failure_reason}\",\n        f\"  Output file: {step.output_file}\",\n        file_info.rstrip(),\n        f\"  Step timeout: {step.timeout_seconds}s | Elapsed: {elapsed}\",\n        \"\",\n        f\"Completed steps: {', '.join(f'{r.step.id} (PASS, attempt {r.attempt})' for r in passed) or 'none'}\",\n        f\"Failed step:     {step.id} ({fail.status.value}, attempt {fail.attempt})\",\n    ]\n\n    # Collect skipped steps\n    all_step_ids = _get_all_step_ids(config)\n    executed_ids = {r.step.id for r in results}\n    skipped_ids = [sid for sid in all_step_ids if sid not in executed_ids]\n    if cancelled:\n        skipped_ids = [r.step.id for r in cancelled] + skipped_ids\n\n    if skipped_ids:\n        lines.append(f\"Skipped steps:   {', '.join(skipped_ids)}\")\n\n    lines.extend(\n        [\n            \"\",\n            \"To retry from this step:\",\n            f\"  superclaude roadmap run {config.spec_file} _get_all_step_ids(config: RoadmapConfig) -> list[str]:\n    \"\"\"Get all step IDs in pipeline order.\"\"\"\n    agent_a = config.agents[0]\n    agent_b = config.agents[1] if len(config.agents) > 1 else config.agents[0]\n    return [\n        \"extract\",\n        f\"generate-{agent_a.id}\",\n        f\"generate-{agent_b.id}\",\n        \"diff\",\n        \"debate\",\n        \"score\",\n        \"merge\",\n        \"anti-instinct\",\n        \"test-strategy\",\n        \"spec-fidelity\",\n        \"wiring-verification\",\n        \"remediate\",\n        \"certify\",\n    ]\n\n\ndef _print_terminal_halt(\n    output_dir: Path,\n    remaining_findings: list,\n    attempt_count: int,\n    spec_patch_budget_exhausted: bool = False,\n    file=None,\n) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Print terminal halt message to stderr with finding details (SC-6).\n\n    Outputs:\n    - Attempt count and remaining failing finding count\n    - Per-finding details (ID, severity, description)\n    - Manual-fix instructions including certification report path and resume command\n\n    Args:\n        output_dir: Pipeline output directory (for certification report path)\n        remaining_findings: List of Finding objects that failed remediation\n        attempt_count: Number of remediation attempts made\n        spec_patch_budget_exhausted: If True, note that spec-patch budget is also exhausted\n        file: Output stream (defaults to sys.stderr)\n    \"\"\"\n    if file is None:\n        file = sys.stderr\n\n    certify_path = output_dir / \"certify.md\"\n\n    lines = [\n        \"\",\n        \"=\" * 72,\n        \"TERMINAL HALT: Remediation budget exhausted\",\n        \"=\" * 72,\n        f\"Attempt count: {attempt_count}\",\n        f\"Remaining failing findings: {len(remaining_findings)}\",\n        \"\",\n    ]\n\n    if remaining_findings:\n        lines.append(\"Failing findings:\")\n        for finding in remaining_findings:\n            severity = getattr(finding, \"severity\", \"UNKNOWN\")\n            description = getattr(finding, \"description\", \"\")\n            finding_id = getattr(finding, \"id\", \"UNKNOWN\")\n            lines.append(f\"  - {finding_id} [{severity}]: {description}\")\n        lines.append(\"\")\n\n    lines.extend(\n        [\n            \"Manual fix required:\",\n            f\"  1. Review certification report: {certify_path}\",\n            \"  2. Fix remaining findings manually\",\n            \"  3. Resume pipeline with:\",\n            f\"     superclaude roadmap run --resume\",\n            \"\",\n        ]\n    )\n\n    if spec_patch_budget_exhausted:\n        lines.extend(\n            [\n                \"Note: Both the remediation budget and the spec-patch cycle budget\",\n                \"are exhausted. Full dual-budget recovery is deferred to v2.26.\",\n                \"# TODO(v2.26): implement dual-budget-exhaustion recovery mechanism\",\n                \"\",\n            ]\n        )\n\n    lines.append(\"=\" * 72)\n\n    print(\"\\n\".join(lines), file=file, flush=True)\n\n\ndef _check_annotate_deviations_freshness(\n    output_dir: Path,\n    roadmap_file: Path,\n    gate_pass_state: dict[str, bool] | None = None,\n) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Check if spec-deviations.md hash matches current roadmap.md (SC-8).\n\n    Reads roadmap_hash from spec-deviations.md frontmatter and compares\n    against sha256(roadmap.md). Fail-closed for all error conditions.\n\n    On hash mismatch, resets spec-fidelity and deviation-analysis gate\n    pass state to force re-run (FR-084).\n\n    Returns:\n        True if hash matches (fresh), False for any failure or mismatch.\n    \"\"\"\n    spec_deviations = output_dir / \"spec-deviations.md\"\n\n    # Case 1: spec-deviations.md not found\n    if not spec_deviations.exists():\n        _log.warning(\"Freshness check: spec-deviations.md not found\")\n        return False\n\n    # Case 2: Read error\n    try:\n        content = spec_deviations.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    except OSError as e:\n        _log.warning(\"Freshness check: read error for spec-deviations.md: %s\", e)\n        return False\n\n    # Case 3: Empty file\n    if not content.strip():\n        _log.warning(\"Freshness check: spec-deviations.md is empty\")\n        return False\n\n    # Case 4: Corrupt/missing frontmatter\n    stripped = content.lstrip()\n    if not stripped.startswith(\"---\"):\n        _log.warning(\"Freshness check: spec-deviations.md has no frontmatter\")\n        return False\n\n    rest = stripped[3:].lstrip(\"\\n\")\n    end_idx = rest.find(\"\\n---\")\n    if end_idx == -1:\n        _log.warning(\"Freshness check: spec-deviations.md has corrupt frontmatter\")\n        return False\n\n    # Parse roadmap_hash from frontmatter\n    saved_hash: str | None = None\n    for line in rest[:end_idx].splitlines():\n        line = line.strip()\n        if line.startswith(\"roadmap_hash:\"):\n            saved_hash = line.split(\":\", 1)[1].strip()\n            break\n\n    # Case 5: roadmap_hash field missing or empty\n    if not saved_hash:\n        _log.warning(\n            \"Freshness check: roadmap_hash field missing or empty in spec-deviations.md\"\n        )\n        return False\n\n    # Case 6: roadmap.md not found\n    if not roadmap_file.exists():\n        _log.warning(\"Freshness check: roadmap.md not found at %s\", roadmap_file)\n        return False\n\n    # Case 7: roadmap.md read error\n    try:\n        roadmap_content = roadmap_file.read_bytes()\n    except OSError as e:\n        _log.warning(\"Freshness check: read error for roadmap.md: %s\", e)\n        return False\n\n    # Case 8: Hash comparison\n    current_hash = hashlib.sha256(roadmap_content).hexdigest()\n    if saved_hash != current_hash:\n        _log.warning(\n            \"Freshness check: hash mismatch -- saved=%s current=%s\",\n            saved_hash[:12],\n            current_hash[:12],\n        )\n        # FR-084: reset gate pass state for downstream steps\n        if gate_pass_state is not None:\n            for key in (\"spec-fidelity\", \"deviation-analysis\"):\n                if key in gate_pass_state:\n                    gate_pass_state[key] = False\n        return False\n\n    return True\n\n\ndef _check_remediation_budget(\n    output_dir: Path,\n    max_attempts: int = 2,\n    halt_fn: \"Callable[[Path, list, int], None] | None\" = None,\n) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Check if remediation budget allows another attempt (SC-6).\n\n    Reads remediation_attempts from .roadmap-state.json.\n    If attempts >= max_attempts, calls halt_fn (or _print_terminal_halt)\n    and returns False.\n\n    Non-integer remediation_attempts is coerced to 0 with a WARNING log.\n\n    Args:\n        output_dir: Pipeline output directory containing .roadmap-state.json\n        max_attempts: Maximum allowed remediation attempts (default 2)\n        halt_fn: Optional callable for terminal halt; defaults to _print_terminal_halt\n\n    Returns:\n        True if budget allows another attempt, False if exhausted.\n    \"\"\"\n    state_file = output_dir / \".roadmap-state.json\"\n    state = read_state(state_file)\n\n    attempts = 0\n    if state is not None:\n        raw = state.get(\"remediation_attempts\", 0)\n        try:\n            attempts = int(raw)\n        except (ValueError, TypeError):\n            _log.warning(\"Non-integer remediation_attempts %r coerced to 0\", raw)\n            attempts = 0\n\n    if attempts >= max_attempts:\n        if halt_fn is not None:\n            halt_fn(output_dir, [], attempts + 1)\n        else:\n            _print_terminal_halt(\n                output_dir=output_dir,\n                remaining_findings=[],\n                attempt_count=attempts + 1,\n            )\n        return False\n\n    return True\n\n\ndef _print_step_start(step: Step) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Print progress output when a step starts.\"\"\"\n    print(f\"[roadmap] Starting step: {step.id}\", flush=True)\n\n\ndef _print_step_complete(step: Step, result: StepResult) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Print progress output when a step completes.\"\"\"\n       flush=True,\n        )\n    else:\n        print(\n            f\"[roadmap] Step {step.id}  {result.status.value} (attempt {result.attempt}, {duration})\",\n            flush=True,\n        )\n        if result.gate_failure_reason:\n            print(f\"           Reason: {result.gate_failure_reason}\", flush=True)\n\n\ndef _dry_run_output(steps: list[Step | list[Step]]) -> None:\n ``remediate``,\n    and ``certify`` keys if present.          )\n                return\n\n    existing_validation = existing.get(\"validation\") if existing else None\n    existing_fidelity = existing.get(\"fidelity_status\") if existing else None\n spec-fidelity StepResult.\n\n    Returns one of: 'pass', 'fail', 'skipped', 'degraded'.\n    \"\"\"\n    if result.status == StepStatus.PASS:\n        # Check if the output indicates degraded mode\n     \"tasklist_ready: false\\n\"\n        \"---\\n\"\n        \"\\n\"\n        \"## Degraded Fidelity Report\\n\"\n        \"\\n\"\n        \"Spec-fidelity validation could not be completed.\\n\"\n derive_pipeline_status(state: dict) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Derive the overall pipeline status from state transitions.\n\n    State transitions at each boundary:\n    - post-validate: validated | 'remediated', 'certified', 'certified-with-caveats'.\n    \"\"\"\n    certify = state.get(\"certify\")\n    if certify is not None:\n        if certify.get(\"certified\", False):\n            return except (json.JSONDecodeError, OSError):\n        return None\n\n\ndef apply_decomposition_pass(deliverables: list[Deliverable]) -> list[Deliverable]:\n    \"\"\"Post-generation decomposition pass for depth_explicit: bool,\n) -> RoadmapConfig:\n    \"\"\"Restore agent/depth specs from .roadmap-state.json when not explicit.\n\n    On --resume, if the user did not explicitly pass --agents or --depth,\n    restore the values from the state file so the pipeline uses the same\n    configuration as the original run.\n    \"\"\"\n    state_file = config.output_dir / \".roadmap-state.json\"\n
