bool = False,\n    no_validate: bool = False,\n    auto_accept: bool = False,\n    agents_explicit: bool = True,\n    depth_explicit: bool = True,\n) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Execute the roadmap generation pipeline.\n\n    Builds the step list, handles --dry-run and --resume, then\n    delegates to execute_pipeline() with roadmap_run_step.\n\n    After all 9 steps pass, auto-invokes validation unless\n    --no-validate is set or --resume halted on a failed step.\n\n    Note: --no-validate does NOT skip the spec-fidelity step\n    (FR-010, AC-005). It only skips the post-pipeline validation\n    subsystem.\n\n    Args:\n        auto_accept: When True, the spec-patch resume cycle skips the\n            interactive prompt and proceeds automatically if evidence is\n            found. When False (default), the cycle prompts the user.\n            This is an internal parameter, not exposed on the CLI.\n        agents_explicit: Whether --agents was explicitly passed on the CLI.\n        depth_explicit: Whether --depth was explicitly passed on the CLI.\n    \"\"\"\n    config.output_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n\n    # On --resume with defaulted agents/depth, restore from state file\n    if resume:\n        config = _restore_from_state(\n            config,\n            agents_explicit=agents_explicit,\n            depth_explicit=depth_explicit,\n        )\n\n    # Apply hardcoded defaults for any still-None fields (non-resume or no state)\n    if not config.agents:\n        config.agents = [AgentSpec(\"opus\", \"architect\"), AgentSpec(\"haiku\", \"architect\")]\n    if not config.depth:\n        config.depth = \"standard\"\n\n    # FR-2.24.1.11: Recursion guard — local variable, per-invocation\n    _spec_patch_cycle_count = 0\n\n    # FR-2.24.1.9 Condition 3: Capture spec hash at function entry\n    initial_spec_hash = hashlib.sha256(config.spec_file.read_bytes()).hexdigest()\n\n    steps = _build_steps(config)\n\n    # --dry-run: print plan and exit\n    if config.dry_run:\n        _dry_run_output(steps)\n        return\n\n    # --resume: check which steps already pass their gates\n    if resume:\n        from ..pipeline.gates import gate_passed\n\n        steps = _apply_resume(steps, config, gate_passed)\n\n    # Execute pipeline\n    results = execute_pipeline(\n        steps=steps,\n        config=config,\n        run_step=roadmap_run_step,\n        on_step_start=_print_step_start,\n        on_step_complete=_print_step_complete,\n    )\n\n    # Save state\n    _save_state(config, results)\n\n    # Check for failures\n    failures = [r for r in results if r.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT)]\n    if failures:\n        # FR-2.24.1.9: Check if spec-fidelity failed and auto-resume is possible\n        spec_fidelity_failed = any(\n            r.step\n            and r.step.id == \"spec-fidelity\"\n            and r.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT)\n            for r in results\n        )\n\n        if spec_fidelity_failed:\n            resumed = _apply_resume_after_spec_patch(\n                config=config,\n                results=results,\n                auto_accept=auto_accept,\n                initial_spec_hash=initial_spec_hash,\n                cycle_count=_spec_patch_cycle_count,\n            )\n            if resumed:\n                _spec_patch_cycle_count += 1\n                # Cycle complete — resumed pipeline ran to completion or failure\n                # inside _apply_resume_after_spec_patch. If it returned True,\n                # we're done (either success or failure was handled internally).\n                return\n\n        halt_msg = _format_halt_output(results, config)\n        print(halt_msg, file=sys.stderr)\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    print(f\"\\n[roadmap] Pipeline complete: {len(results)} steps passed\", flush=True)\n\n    # Auto-invoke validation after successful pipeline completion\n    if no_validate:\n        print(\"[roadmap] Validation skipped (--no-validate)\", flush=True)\n        _save_validation_status(config, \"skipped\")\n        return\n\n    # Check if validation already completed (--resume path)\n    if resume:\n        state_file = config.output_dir / \".roadmap-state.json\"\n        state = read_state(state_file)\n        if state and \"validation\" in state:\n            saved = state[\"validation\"]\n            if saved.get(\"status\") in (\"pass\", \"fail\"):\n                print(\n                    f\"[roadmap] Validation already completed ({saved['status']}), skipping\",\n                    flush=True,\n                )\n                return\n\n    _auto_invoke_validate(config)\n\n\ndef _find_qualifying_deviation_files(\n    config: RoadmapConfig,\n    results: list[StepResult],\n) -> list:\n    \"\"\"Find deviation files written after spec-fidelity started.\n\n    Returns qualifying DeviationRecord objects, or empty list if\n    conditions are not met.\n\n    Implementation detail — not specified in the spec. Extracted for\n    testability of the three-condition detection gate.\n    \"\"\"\n    from .spec_patch import scan_accepted_deviation_records\n\n    state_file = config.output_dir / \".roadmap-state.json\"\n    state = read_state(state_file)\n    if state is None:\n        return []\n\n    # Get spec-fidelity started_at timestamp\n    steps_state = state.get(\"steps\", {})\n    fidelity_state = steps_state.get(\"spec-fidelity\", {})\n    started_at_str = fidelity_state.get(\"started_at\")\n\n    # Fail-closed: if started_at is absent, condition not met\n    if not started_at_str:\n        return []\n\n    try:\n        started_at_ts = datetime.fromisoformat(started_at_str).timestamp()\n    except (ValueError, TypeError):\n        return []\n\n    # Scan all deviation records\n    all_records = scan_accepted_deviation_records(config.output_dir)\n    if not all_records:\n        return []\n\n    # Filter to records written AFTER spec-fidelity started.\n    # Strict > (not >=): a record with mtime == started_at was written before\n    # or exactly at step start, so it cannot be evidence of a subprocess fix.\n    # Caveat: HFS+ and some NFS mounts have 1-second mtime resolution, so\n    # records created within the same second as started_at may be missed.\n    qualifying = [r for r in all_records if r.mtime > started_at_ts]\n    return qualifying\n\n\ndef _apply_resume_after_spec_patch(\n    config: RoadmapConfig,\n    results: list[StepResult],\n    auto_accept: bool,\n    initial_spec_hash: str,\n    cycle_count: int,\n) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Attempt a single spec-patch auto-resume cycle after spec-fidelity FAIL.\n\n    Evaluates the three-condition detection gate (FR-2.24.1.9):\n      1. Recursion guard: cycle_count == 0\n      2. Qualifying deviation files exist with mtime > started_at\n      3. Spec file hash changed since run started (initial_spec_hash)\n\n    If all conditions pass, executes the six-step disk-reread sequence\n    (FR-2.24.1.10) and re-runs the pipeline via _apply_resume.\n\n    Single-writer assumption: no concurrent writer modifies\n    .roadmap-state.json between the reread and write steps.\n\n    Returns True if the cycle was attempted (regardless of outcome),\n    False if conditions were not met.\n    \"\"\"\n    # FR-2.24.1.11: Recursion guard\n    if cycle_count >= 1:\n        print(\n            \"[roadmap] Spec-patch cycle already exhausted \"\n            f\"(cycle_count={cycle_count}). Proceeding to normal failure.\",\n            flush=True,\n        )\n        return False\n\n    # FR-2.24.1.9 Condition 2: Qualifying deviation files\n    qualifying = _find_qualifying_deviation_files(config, results)\n    if not qualifying:\n        return False\n\n    # FR-2.24.1.9 Condition 3: Spec hash changed since run started\n    current_hash = hashlib.sha256(config.spec_file.read_bytes()).hexdigest()\n    if current_hash == initial_spec_hash:\n        return False\n\n    # All three conditions met — enter the cycle\n    # FR-2.24.1.12: Cycle entry logging\n    print(\n        f\"[roadmap] Spec patched by subprocess. \"\n        f\"Found {len(qualifying)} accepted deviation record(s).\",\n        flush=True,\n    )\n    print(\n        \"[roadmap] Triggering spec-hash sync and resume (cycle 1/1).\",\n        flush=True,\n    )\n\n    # FR-2.24.1.10: Six-step disk-reread sequence\n    state_file = config.output_dir / \".roadmap-state.json\"\n\n    # Step 1: Re-read state from disk\n    _fresh_state = read_state(state_file)  # noqa: F841\n\n    # Step 2: Recompute spec hash\n    new_hash = hashlib.sha256(config.spec_file.read_bytes()).hexdigest()\n\n    # Step 3: Atomic write of new hash\n    try:\n        # Read again for fresh copy, update only spec_hash, write atomically\n        fresh_for_write = read_state(state_file) or {}\n        fresh_for_write[\"spec_hash\"] = new_hash\n        write_state(fresh_for_write, state_file)\n    except OSError as exc:\n        print(\n            f\"[roadmap] ERROR: Failed to update spec_hash during \"\n            f\"auto-resume cycle: {exc}. Falling through to normal failure.\",\n            file=sys.stderr,\n            flush=True,\n        )\n        return True  # Cycle was attempted but failed — don't retry\n\n    # Step 4: Re-read state from disk AGAIN (this is what _apply_resume gets)\n    post_write_state = read_state(state_file)\n    if post_write_state is None:\n        print(\n            \"[roadmap] ERROR: Could not re-read state after write. \"\n            \"Falling through to normal failure.\",\n            file=sys.stderr,\n            flush=True,\n        )\n        return True\n\n    # Step 5: Rebuild steps\n    steps = _build_steps(config)\n\n    # Step 6: Apply resume with post-write state\n    from ..pipeline.gates import gate_passed\n\n    steps = _apply_resume(steps, config, gate_passed)\n\n    # Re-execute pipeline from the resumed point\n    resumed_results = execute_pipeline(\n        steps=steps,\n        config=config,\n        run_step=roadmap_run_step,\n        on_step_start=_print_step_start,\n        on_step_complete=_print_step_complete,\n    )\n\n    # FR-2.24.1.13: Normal failure on cycle exhaustion\n        # Use second-run results only\n        halt_msg = _format_halt_output(resumed_results, config)\n        print(halt_msg, file=sys.stderr)\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    # Any of its input files are in the dirty set, OR\n    3. Its own gate check fails (using state-recorded paths when available).\n\n    Returns:\n        (needs_rerun: bool, reason: str)\n    \"\"\"\n    if force_extract and step.id == \"extract\":\n        return True, \"spec file changed; forcing extract rerun\"\n\n    # If any input was re-generated, must re-run\n    if any(inp in dirty_outputs for inp in (step.inputs or [])):\n        deps = [str(inp) for inp in (step.inputs or []) if inp in dirty_outputs]\n        return True, f\"input dependency regenerated: {deps}\"\n\n    # Defense-in-depth: use state-recorded path for gate check\n    check_path = state_paths.get(step.id, step.output_file)\n    if check_path != step.output_file:\n        _log.info(\n            \"Resume: step '%s' using state-recorded path %s \"\n            \"(config-derived: %s)\",\n            step.id,\n            check_path,\n            step.output_file,\n        )\n\n    # Check own gate\n    if step.gate:\n        passed, reason = gate_fn(check_path, step.gate)\n        if passed:\n            return False, \"gate passes\"\n        # Log the failure reason with diagnostic hint\n        if reason and \"File not found\" in reason:\n            print(\n                f\"[roadmap] {step.id}: output missing ({check_path.name})\\n\"\n                f\"  Hint: Were different --agents used in the original run?\",\n                file=sys.stderr,\n                flush=True,\n            )\n        else:\n            print(f\"[roadmap] {step.id}: gate failed -- {reason}\", flush=True)\n        return True, f\"gate failed: {reason}\"\n\n    # No gate defined -- must run\n    return True, \"no gate defined\"\n\n\ndef _apply_resume(\n    steps: list[Step | list[Step]],\n    config: RoadmapConfig,\n    gate_fn: Callable,\n) -> list[Step | list[Step]]:\n    \"\"\"Apply --resume logic: skip steps whose outputs pass gates.\n\n    Uses dependency tracking: if a step's inputs include the output of a\n    step that will be re-run, it must also re-run regardless of gate status.\n\n    Includes state-driven path resolution and parallel group semantics.\n    \"\"\"\n    state_file = config.output_dir / \".roadmap-state.json\"\n    state = read_state(state_file)\n    force_extract = False\n\n    # State-driven path resolution: build lookup step_id -> recorded output_file\n    state_paths: dict[str, Path] = {}\n    if state is not None:\n        saved_hash = state.get(\"spec_hash\", \"\")\n        current_hash = hashlib.sha256(config.spec_file.read_bytes()).hexdigest()\n        if saved_hash and saved_hash != current_hash:\n            print(\n                f\"WARNING: spec-file has changed since last run.\\n\"\n                f\"  Last hash: {saved_hash[:12]}...\\n\"\n                f\"  Current:   {current_hash[:12]}...\\n\"\n                f\"Forcing re-run of extract step.\",\n                file=sys.stderr,\n                flush=True,\n            )\n            force_extract = True\n\n        # Extract recorded output paths from state\n        for step_id, step_data in state.get(\"steps\", {}).items():\n            recorded_path = step_data.get(\"output_file\")\n            if recorded_path:\n                state_paths[step_id] = Path(recorded_path)\n\n    skipped = 0\n    result: list[Step | list[Step]] = []\n    dirty_outputs: set[Path] = set()  # files that will be regenerated\n\n    for entry in steps:\n        if isinstance(entry, list):\n            # Parallel group: check each step, re-run entire group if any needs it\n            group_needs_rerun = False\n            rerun_reasons: list[str] = []\n\n            for s in entry:\n                needs, reason = _step_needs_rerun(\n                    s, gate_fn, dirty_outputs, force_extract, state_paths,\n                )\n                if needs:\n                    group_needs_rerun = True\n                    rerun_reasons.append(f\"{s.id}: {reason}\")\n\n            if group_needs_rerun:\n                _log.info(\n                    \"Parallel group [%s] marked for rerun: %s\",\n                    \", \".join(s.id for s in entry),\n                    \"; \".join(rerun_reasons),\n                )\n                result.append(entry)\n                # Mark all group outputs as dirty (atomic group completion)\n                for s in entry:\n                    dirty_outputs.add(s.output_file)\n            else:\n                skipped += len(entry)\n                print(\n                    f\"[roadmap] Skipping {', '.join(s.id for s in entry)} (gates pass)\",\n                    flush=True,\n                )\n        else:\n            # Single step\n            needs, reason = _step_needs_rerun(\n                entry, gate_fn, dirty_outputs, force_extract, state_paths,\n            )\n\n            if needs:\n                _log.info(\"Step '%s' marked for rerun: %s\", entry.id, reason)\n                dirty_outputs.add(entry.output_file)\n                result.append(entry)\n            else:\n                skipped += 1\n                print(f\"[roadmap] Skipping {entry.id} (gate passes)\", flush=True)\n\n    if skipped > 0:\n        print(f\"[roadmap] Skipped {skipped} steps (gates pass)\", flush=True)\n\n    if not result:\n        print(\"[roadmap] All steps already pass gates. Nothing to do.\", flush=True)\n\n    return result\n","numLines":2064,"startLine":1,"totalLines":2064}}}

Results are merged by stable ID, and adversarial\n    debate validates each HIGH finding.\n\n    Does NOT perform any ledger operations internally — the caller\n    (execute_fidelity_with_convergence) handles budget debiting.\n\n    Parameters\n    ----------\n    registry : DeviationRegistry\n        The deviation registry (updated with debate verdicts).\n    spec_path : Path\n        Path to spec file.\n    roadmap_path : Path\n        Path to roadmap file.\n\n    Returns\n    -------\n    RegressionResult\n        Consolidated validation result with findings and debate verdicts.\n    \"\"\"\n    dirs = _create_validation_dirs(\n        spec_path, roadmap_path, registry.path, count=3,\n    )\n    try:\n        # All 3 agents must succeed for validation to be considered valid\n        if agents_succeeded < 3:\n            logger.error(\n                \"Regression validation FAILED: only %d/3 agents succeeded\",\n                agents_succeeded,\n            )\n            return RegressionResult(\n                agents_succeeded=agents_succeeded,\n            )\n\n        # Merge results by stable ID: preserve unique findings\n        merged: dict[str, dict] = {}\n        for agent_findings in agent_results:\n            for sid, finding in agent_findings.items():\n                if sid not in merged:\n                    merged[sid] = finding\n\n        # Sort by severity: HIGH -> MEDIUM -> LOW\n        severity_order = {\"HIGH\": 0, \"MEDIUM\": 1, \"LOW\": 2}\n        validated = sorted(\n            merged.values(),\n            key=lambda f: severity_order.get(f.get(\"severity\", \"LOW\"), 3),\n        )\n\n        # Signature: (registry, spec_path, roadmap_path) -> RegressionResult.","+    max_runs : int","+        Maximum number of checker runs (default 3).","+    spec_path : Path | None","+        Path to spec file (for regression validation).","+    roadmap_path : Path | None","+        Path to roadmap file (for regression validation).","+","+    Returns","+    -------","+    ConvergenceResult","+        Outcome including pass/fail, run count, and diagnostic logs.","+    \"\"\"","+    run_labels = [\"catch\", \"verify\", \"backup\"]","+    structural_progress: list[str] = []","+    semantic_fluctuation: list[str] = []","+    prev_structural_highs = registry.get_structural_high_count()","+","+    for run_idx in range(max_runs):","+        run_label = run_labels[run_idx] if run_idx < len(run_labels) else f\"run-{run_idx + 1}\"","+","+        # Budget guard: can we afford a checker run?","+        if not ledger.can_launch():","+            halt_msg = (","+                f\"Budget exhausted before run {run_idx + 1} ({run_label}). \"","+                f\"TurnLedger: available={ledger.available()}, \"","+                f\"consumed={ledger.consumed}, initial={ledger.initial_budget}\"","+            )","+            logger.error(halt_msg)","+            return ConvergenceResult(","+                passed=False,","+                run_count=run_idx,","+                final_high_count=registry.get_active_high_count(),","+                structural_progress_log=structural_progress,","+                semantic_fluctuation_log=semantic_fluctuation,","+                halt_reason=halt_msg,","+            )","+","+        # Debit for checker run","+        ledger.debit(CHECKER_COST)","+        run_number = registry.begin_run(","+            roadmap_hash=hashlib.sha256(","+                (roadmap_path.read_bytes() if roadmap_path and roadmap_path.exists() else b\"\")","+            ).hexdigest()","+        )","+","+        # Execute checkers","+        run_checkers(registry, run_number)","+","+        # Check pass condition","+        active_highs = registry.get_active_high_count()","+        curr_structural = registry.get_structural_high_count()","+        curr_semantic = registry.get_semantic_high_count()","+","+        if active_highs == 0:","+            ledger.credit(CONVERGENCE_PASS_CREDIT)","+            logger.info(","+                \"Run %d (%s): PASS — 0 active HIGHs. Credit %d turns.\",","+                run_idx + 1, run_label, CONVERGENCE_PASS_CREDIT,","+            )","+            return ConvergenceResult(","+                passed=True,","+                run_count=run_idx + 1,","+                final_high_count=0,","+                structural_progress_log=structural_progress,","+                semantic_fluctuation_log=semantic_fluctuation,","+            )","+","+        # Log progress","+        progress_msg = (","+            f\"Run {run_idx + 1} ({run_label}): structural {prev_structural_highs} -> {curr_structural}\"","+        )","+        structural_progress.append(progress_msg)","+","+        # Check for semantic fluctuation","+        prev_semantic = (","+            registry.runs[-2].get(\"semantic_high_count\", 0)","+            if len(registry.runs) >= 2 else 0","+        )","+        if curr_semantic != prev_semantic:","+            fluct_msg = (","+                f\"Run {run_idx + 1}: semantic HIGH fluctuation \"","+                f\"{prev_semantic} -> {curr_semantic} (warning only)\"","+            )","+            semantic_fluctuation.append(fluct_msg)","+            logger.warning(fluct_msg)","+","+        # Check for structural regression","+        if curr_structural > prev_structural_highs:","+            logger.error(","+                \"Structural regression in run %d: %d -> %d\",","+                run_idx + 1, prev_structural_highs, curr_structural,","+            )","+            if handle_regression_fn and spec_path and roadmap_path:","+                # Budget guard for regression validation","+                if not ledger.can_launch():","+                    halt_msg = (","+                        f\"Budget exhausted before regression validation. \"","+                        f\"TurnLedger: available={ledger.available()}\"","+                    )","+                    return ConvergenceResult(","+                        passed=False,","+                        run_count=run_idx + 1,","+                        final_high_count=active_highs,","+                        structural_progress_log=structural_progress,","+                        semantic_fluctuation_log=semantic_fluctuation,","+                        regression_detected=True,","+                        halt_reason=halt_msg,","+                    )","+                ledger.debit(REGRESSION_VALIDATION_COST)","+                handle_regression_fn(registry, spec_path, roadmap_path)","+                # Re-evaluate after regression handling","+                active_highs = registry.get_active_high_count()","+                curr_structural = registry.get_structural_high_count()","+","+            return ConvergenceResult(","+                passed=False,","+                run_count=run_idx + 1,","+                final_high_count=active_highs,","+                structural_progress_log=structural_progress,","+                semantic_fluctuation_log=semantic_fluctuation,","+                regression_detected=True,","+            )","+","+        # Remediate before next run (if not the last run)","+        if run_idx < max_runs - 1:","+            if not ledger.can_remediate():","+                halt_msg = (","+                    f\"Budget exhausted before remediation after run {run_idx + 1}. \"","+                    f\"TurnLedger: available={ledger.available()}\"","+                )","+                logger.error(halt_msg)","+                return ConvergenceResult(","+                    passed=False,","+                    run_count=run_idx + 1,","+                    final_high_count=active_highs,","+                    structural_progress_log=structural_progress,","+                    semantic_fluctuation_log=semantic_fluctuation,","+                    halt_reason=halt_msg,","+                )","+            ledger.debit(REMEDIATION_COST)","+            run_remediation(registry)","+","+        registry.save()","+","+    # All runs exhausted without convergence","+    final_highs = registry.get_active_high_count()","+    halt_msg = (","+        f\"Convergence not reached after {max_runs} runs. \"","+        f\"Remaining active HIGHs: {final_highs}. \"","+        f\"TurnLedger: available={ledger.available()}, consumed={ledger.consumed}\"","+    )","+    logger.error(halt_msg)","+    return ConvergenceResult(","+        passed=False,","+        run_count=max_runs,","+        final_high_count=final_highs,","+        structural_progress_log=structural_progress,","+        semantic_fluctuation_log=semantic_fluctuation,","+        halt_reason=halt_msg,","+    )","+","+","+def handle_regression(","+    registry: DeviationRegistry,","+    spec_path: Path,","+    roadmap_path: Path,","+) -> RegressionResult:","+    \"\"\"Handle structural regression via parallel validation (FR-8).","+","+    Spawns 3 agents in isolated temp dirs, each running the full checker","+    suite independently. Results are merged by stable ID, and adversarial","+    debate validates each HIGH finding.","+","+    Does NOT perform any ledger operations internally — the caller","+    (execute_fidelity_with_convergence) handles budget debiting.","+","+    Parameters","+    ----------","+    registry : DeviationRegistry","+        The deviation registry (updated with debate verdicts).","+    spec_path : Path","+        Path to spec file.","+    roadmap_path : Path","+        Path to roadmap file.","+","+    Returns","+    -------","+    RegressionResult","+        Consolidated validation result with findings and debate verdicts.","+    \"\"\"","+    dirs = _create_validation_dirs(","+        spec_path, roadmap_path, registry.path, count=3,","+    )","+    try:","+        # Merge results by stable ID: preserve unique findings","+        merged: dict[str, dict] = {}","+        for agent_findings in agent_results:","+            for sid, finding in agent_findings.items():","+                if sid not in merged:","+                    merged[sid] = finding","+","+        # prev_structural:\n        logger.error(\n            \"Structural regression detected: %d -> %d HIGHs\",\n            prev_structural, curr_structural,\n        )\n        return True\n\n    return False\n\n\n_active_validation_dirs: list[Path] = []\n\n\ndef _create_validation_dirs(\n    spec_path: Path,\n    roadmap_path: Path,\n    registry_path: Path,\n    count: int = 3,\n) -> list[Path]:\n    \"\"\"Create temporary directories with independent file copies.\n\n    Each directory gets its own copy of spec, roadmap, and registry.\n    Replaces git worktrees (BF-4: checkers don't need git repo).\n    \"\"\"\n    dirs: list[Path] = []\n    for i in range(count):\n        d = Path(tempfile.mkdtemp(prefix=f\"fidelity-validation-{i}-\"))\n        shutil.copy2(spec_path, d / spec_path.name)\n        shutil.copy2(roadmap_path, d / roadmap_path.name)\n        if registry_path.exists():\n            shutil.copy2(registry_path, d / registry_path.name)\n        dirs.append(d)\n\n    _active_validation_dirs.extend(dirs)\n    return dirs\n\n\ndef _cleanup_validation_dirs(dirs: list[Path]) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Remove temporary validation directories.\n\n    Best-effort cleanup: logs warning on failure, does not raise.\n    \"\"\"\n    for d in dirs:\n        try:\n            shutil.rmtree(d)\n            if d in _active_validation_dirs:\n                _active_validation_dirs.remove(d)\n        except OSError as exc:\n            logger.warning(\"Failed to clean up validation dir %s: %s\", d, exc)\n\n\ndef _atexit_cleanup() -> None:\n    \"\"\"Fallback cleanup registered with atexit.\"\"\"\n    if _active_validation_dirs:\n        logger.info(\"atexit: cleaning up %d validation dirs\", len(_active_validation_dirs))\n        _cleanup_validation_dirs(list(_active_validation_dirs))\n\n\natexit.register(_atexit_cleanup)\n\n\ndef execute_fidelity_with_convergence(\n    registry: DeviationRegistry,\n    ledger,\n    run_checkers: \"Callable\",\n    run_remediation: \"Callable\",\n    handle_regression_fn: \"Callable | None\" = None,\n    max_runs: int = 3,\n    spec_path: Path | None = None,\n    roadmap_path: Path | None = None,\n) -> ConvergenceResult:\n    \"\"\"Convergence-controlled fidelity gate (FR-7).\n\n    Coordinates up to max_runs (default 3) checker/remediation cycles\n    within step 8 with TurnLedger budget accounting.\n\n    Run labels: Run 1 (catch) -> remediation -> Run 2 (verify) -> remediation -> Run 3 (backup).\n\n    Pass condition: registry.get_active_high_count() == 0.\n    Monotonic progress enforced on structural_high_count only.\n    Semantic HIGH fluctuations logged as warnings.\n    Budget exhaustion halts with diagnostic report.\n\n    Parameters\n    ----------\n    registry : DeviationRegistry\n        The deviation registry tracking findings across runs.\n    ledger : TurnLedger\n        Budget accounting object (from sprint.models).\n    run_checkers : Callable\n        Function that runs structural + semantic checkers and merges\n        findings into the registry. Signature: (registry, run_number) -> None.\n    run_remediation : Callable\n        Function that attempts to remediate active HIGH findings.\n        Signature: (registry) -> None.\n    handle_regression_fn : Callable | None\n        Function to handle regression detection. Called when structural\n        HIGHs increase. Signature: (registry, spec_path, roadmap_path) -> RegressionResult.\n    max_runs : int\n        Maximum number of checker runs (default 3).\n    spec_path : Path | None\n        Path to spec file (for regression validation).\n    roadmap_path : Path | None\n        Path to roadmap file (for regression validation).\n\n    Returns\n    -------\n    ConvergenceResult\n        Outcome including pass/fail, run count, and diagnostic logs.\n    \"\"\"\n    run_labels = [\"catch\", \"verify\", \"backup\"]\n    structural_progress: list[str] = []\n    semantic_fluctuation: list[str] = []\n    prev_structural_highs = registry.get_structural_high_count()\n\n    for run_idx in range(max_runs):\n        run_label = run_labels[run_idx] if run_idx < len(run_labels) else f\"run-{run_idx + 1}\"\n\n        # Budget guard: can we afford a checker run?\n        if not ledger.can_launch():\n            halt_msg = (\n                f\"Budget exhausted before run {run_idx + 1} ({run_label}). \"\n                f\"TurnLedger: available={ledger.available()}, \"\n                f\"consumed={ledger.consumed}, initial={ledger.initial_budget}\"\n            )\n            logger.error(halt_msg)\n            return ConvergenceResult(\n                passed=False,\n                run_count=run_idx,\n                final_high_count=registry.get_active_high_count(),\n                structural_progress_log=structural_progress,\n                semantic_fluctuation_log=semantic_fluctuation,\n                halt_reason=halt_msg,\n            )\n\n        # Debit for checker run\n        ledger.debit(CHECKER_COST)\n        run_number = registry.begin_run(\n            roadmap_hash=hashlib.sha256(\n                (roadmap_path.read_bytes() if roadmap_path and roadmap_path.exists() else b\"\")\n            ).hexdigest()\n        )\n\n        # Execute checkers\n        run_checkers(registry, run_number)\n\n        # Check pass condition\n        active_highs = registry.get_active_high_count()\n        curr_structural = registry.get_structural_high_count()\n        curr_semantic = registry.get_semantic_high_count()\n\n        if active_highs == 0:\n            ledger.credit(CONVERGENCE_PASS_CREDIT)\n            logger.info(\n                \"Run %d (%s): PASS — 0 active HIGHs. Credit %d turns.\",\n                run_idx + 1, run_label, CONVERGENCE_PASS_CREDIT,\n            )\n            return ConvergenceResult(\n                passed=True,\n                run_count=run_idx + 1,\n                final_high_count=0,\n                structural_progress_log=structural_progress,\n                semantic_fluctuation_log=semantic_fluctuation,\n            )\n\n        # Log progress\n        progress_msg = (\n            f\"Run {run_idx + 1} ({run_label}): structural {prev_structural_highs} -> {curr_structural}\"\n        )\n        structural_progress.append(progress_msg)\n\n        # Check for semantic fluctuation\n        prev_semantic = (\n            registry.runs[-2].get(\"semantic_high_count\", 0)\n            if len(registry.runs) >= 2 else 0\n        )\n        if curr_semantic != prev_semantic:\n            fluct_msg = (\n                f\"Run {run_idx + 1}: semantic HIGH fluctuation \"\n                f\"{prev_semantic} -> {curr_semantic} (warning only)\"\n            )\n            semantic_fluctuation.append(fluct_msg)\n            logger.warning(fluct_msg)\n\n        # Budget guard for regression validation\n                if not ledger.can_launch():\n                    halt_msg = (\n                        f\"Budget exhausted before regression validation. \"\n                        f\"TurnLedger: available={ledger.available()}\"\n                    )\n                    return ConvergenceResult(\n                        passed=False,\n                        run_count=run_idx + 1,\n                        final_high_count=active_highs,\n                        structural_progress_log=structural_progress,\n                        semantic_fluctuation_log=semantic_fluctuation,\n                        regression_detected=True,\n                        halt_reason=halt_msg,\n                    )\n                ledger.debit(REGRESSION_VALIDATION_COST)\n                handle_regression_fn(registry, spec_path, roadmap_path)\n                # Re-evaluate after regression handling\n                active_highs = registry.get_active_high_count()\n                curr_structural = registry.get_structural_high_count()\n\n            return ConvergenceResult(\n                passed=False,\n                run_count=run_idx + 1,\n                final_high_count=active_highs,\n                structural_progress_log=structural_progress,\n                semantic_fluctuation_log=semantic_fluctuation,\n                regression_detected=True,\n            )\n\n        # Reimburse for progress\n        credit = reimburse_for_progress(ledger, prev_structural_highs, curr_structural)\n        if credit > 0:\n            progress_credit_msg = (\n                f\"Run {run_idx + 1}: progress credit {credit} turns \"\n                f\"(structural {prev_structural_highs} -> {curr_structural})\"\n            )\n            logger.info(progress_credit_msg)\n            structural_progress.append(progress_credit_msg)\n\n        prev_structural_highs = curr_structural\n\n        # Remediate before next run (if not the last run)\n        if run_idx < max_runs - 1:\n            if not ledger.can_remediate():\n                halt_msg = (\n                    f\"Budget exhausted before remediation after run {run_idx + 1}. \"\n                    f\"TurnLedger: available={ledger.available()}\"\n                )\n                logger.error(halt_msg)\n                return ConvergenceResult(\n                    passed=False,\n                    run_count=run_idx + 1,\n                    final_high_count=active_highs,\n                    structural_progress_log=structural_progress,\n                    semantic_fluctuation_log=semantic_fluctuation,\n                    halt_reason=halt_msg,\n                )\n            ledger.debit(REMEDIATION_COST)\n            run_remediation(registry)\n\n        registry.save()\n\n    # All runs exhausted without convergence\n    final_highs = registry.get_active_high_count()\n    halt_msg = (\n        f\"Convergence not reached after {max_runs} runs. \"\n        f\"Remaining active HIGHs: {final_highs}. \"\n        f\"TurnLedger: available={ledger.available()}, consumed={ledger.consumed}\"\n    )\n    logger.error(halt_msg)\n    return ConvergenceResult(\n        passed=False,\n        run_count=max_runs,\n        final_high_count=final_highs,\n        structural_progress_log=structural_progress,\n        semantic_fluctuation_log=semantic_fluctuation,\n        halt_reason=halt_msg,\n    )\n\n\ndef handle_regression(\n    registry: DeviationRegistry,\n    spec_path: Path,\n    roadmap_path: Path,\n) -> RegressionResult:\n    \"\"\"Handle structural regression via parallel validation (FR-8).\n\n    Spawns 3 agents in isolated temp dirs, each running the full checker\n    suite independently. simulation integration test ---\n\n\nclass TestThreeRunSimulation:\n    \"\"\"T03.04: End-to-end 3-run registry lifecycle.\"\"\"\n\n    def _make_finding(self, id_str, severity=\"HIGH\", source_layer=\"structural\",\n                       dimension=\"signatures\", location=None):\n        if location is None:\n            location = f\"FR-{id_str}\"\n        return Finding(\n            id=id_str, severity=severity, dimension=dimension,\n            description=f\"finding {id_str}\", location=location,\n            evidence=\"ev\", fix_guidance=\"fix\", status=\"ACTIVE\",\n            source_layer=source_layer,\n        )\n\n    def test_three_run_simulation(self, tmp_path):\n        \"\"\"Registry correctly tracks findings across 3 simulated runs.\"\"\"\n        path = tmp_path / \"registry.json\"\n        reg = DeviationRegistry(path=path, release_id=\"test\", spec_hash=\"abc\")\n\n        # --- Run 1: Seed with structural + semantic findings ---\n        run1 = reg.begin_run(\"road1\")\n        structural_r1 = [\n            self._make_finding(\"STR-001\"),\n            self._make_finding(\"STR-002\"),\n        ]\n        semantic_r1 = [\n            self._make_finding(\"SEM-001\", source_layer=\"semantic\"),\n        ]\n        reg.merge_findings(structural_r1, semantic_r1, run_number=run1)\n\n        assert reg.get_structural_high_count() == 2\n        assert reg.get_semantic_high_count() == 1\n        assert reg.get_active_high_count() == 3\n        assert len(reg.findings) == 3\n        assert reg.runs[-1][\"structural_high_count\"] == 2\n        assert reg.runs[-1][\"semantic_high_count\"] == 1\n        assert reg.runs[-1][\"total_high_count\"] == 3\n\n        # Save and reload to test persistence\n        reg.save()\n        reg = DeviationRegistry.load_or_create(path, \"test\", \"abc\")\n\n        # --- Run 2: STR-002 fixed, SEM-002 added ---\n        run2 = reg.begin_run(\"road2\")\n        structural_r2 = [\n            self._make_finding(\"STR-001\"),  # still present\n            # STR-002 is gone (fixed)\n        ]\n        semantic_r2 = [\n            self._make_finding(\"SEM-001\", source_layer=\"semantic\"),  # still present\n            self._make_finding(\"SEM-002\", source_layer=\"semantic\"),  # new\n        ]\n        reg.merge_findings(structural_r2, semantic_r2, run_number=run2)\n\n        # STR-002 should be FIXED\n        str002 = [f for f in reg.findings.values() if f[\"description\"] == \"finding STR-002\"][0]\n        assert str002[\"status\"] == \"FIXED\"\n\n        # New stable IDs for SEM-002\n        sem002 = [f for f in reg.findings.values() if f[\"description\"] == \"finding SEM-002\"][0]\n        assert sem002[\"first_seen_run\"] == 2\n        assert sem002[\"status\"] == \"ACTIVE\"\n\n        assert reg.get_structural_high_count() == 1\n        assert reg.get_semantic_high_count() == 2\n        assert reg.runs[-1][\"structural_high_count\"] == 1\n        assert reg.runs[-1][\"semantic_high_count\"] == 2\n        assert reg.runs[-1][\"total_high_count\"] == 3\n\n        # Save and reload again\n        reg.save()\n        reg = DeviationRegistry.load_or_create(path, \"test\", \"abc\")\n\n        # --- Run 3: Verify cumulative state ---\n        run3 = reg.begin_run(\"road3\")\n        structural_r3 = [\n            self._make_finding(\"STR-001\"),  # still present\n        ]\n        semantic_r3 = [\n            self._make_finding(\"SEM-001\", source_layer=\"semantic\"),\n            # SEM-002 gone (fixed)\n        ]\n        reg.merge_findings(structural_r3, semantic_r3, run_number=run3)\n\n        # Cumulative checks\n        assert len(reg.findings) == 4  # total unique findings across all runs\n        assert reg.get_structural_high_count() == 1\n        assert reg.get_semantic_high_count() == 1\n        assert reg.runs[-1][\"structural_high_count\"] == 1\n        assert reg.runs[-1][\"semantic_high_count\"] == 1\n        assert reg.runs[-1][\"total_high_count\"] == 2\n\n        # Status checks\n        statuses = {f[\"description\"]: f[\"status\"] for f in reg.findings.values()}\n        assert statuses[\"finding STR-001\"] == \"ACTIVE\"\n        assert statuses[\"finding STR-002\"] == \"FIXED\"\n        assert statuses[\"finding SEM-001\"] == \"ACTIVE\"\n        assert statuses[\"finding SEM-002\"] == \"FIXED\"\n\n        # Verify stable IDs are unique (collision-free)\n        all_ids = list(reg.findings.keys())\n        assert len(all_ids) == len(set(all_ids)), \"Stable ID collision detected\"\n\n        # Verify run metadata completeness\n        assert len(reg.runs) == 3\n        for run in reg.runs:\n            assert \"structural_high_count\" in run\n            assert \"semantic_high_count\" in run\n            assert \"total_high_count\" in run\n\n    def test_three_run_stable_id_consistency(self, tmp_path):\n
